ZUCIYAR MUTUM BIRNINSAWhat a freaking love story
By UmmySaudatSaudat Adam Isah
MAIN CHARACTERS:
~Zahra'u Mukhtar NaAllah ~Najib Ahmad Mekudi
ZAHRA ta kasance matashiyar budurwa ce,me kimanin shekaru ashirin a doron duniyanta,wadda sam bataso ta shagaltar da kanta gun yin ladabi ga rudin zamanin nan namu da qyale qyalen dake qunshe cikinsa,me cikar zati na cikakkiyar budurwar da duk wanda ya daga kai ya kalleta sau daya se yayima kansa kwadayin sake yin tozali da kyakkyawar siffarta,son kowa qin wanda ya rasa,sam hkn besa ta shiga jerin irin matasan yan matan nan masu daurama kansu irin isa da tunqaho marasa ingantaccen tushe ba,ko yasata shagala ko kwadayin ta bijirema bin tsaftataccen tafarkin da addinimmu ya shimfida ba,du ko da salon maganar nan me taken 'mutum tara yake be cika goma ba',amman iya qarfin qoqarin ikonta,take tabukawa don bin dokoki da iyakokin Allah,da taimakon mahaliccinta ya dubi aikinta kuma yake shiga lamuranta cikin jagorancinsa,har ta qere ma sa'anninta,ta ko wace irin kafa ma kuma,fintinkau tai musu,it just comes to her naturally,never tries so hard to be d kind of person she is,just plainly geniune_like,comes from proudly muslim background,family of middle class earners 
NAJIB ya kasance matashin saurayi dan kimanin 29yrs da haihuwa,a go getter,unbendable,vigorously high_octaned terror,meji da zamani da abinda ya qunsa,be banbance tsakanin aya da tsakuwa,fari da baqi,kyakkyawan aiki da mummuna,kawai bin duniyar yake kamar besan ana barinta ba,kamar be san da afkuwan wannan abun da akema laqabi da MUTUWA ba,yake faranta ma rudin zuciyarsa, sau da qafa,batareda burki ko qaqqqautawa ba,zuciyar dake danqare da tafkin shedan(la'anannen bawa)b
    1
uh in some degrees,I've come in terms to labell him as an eligible youth,dan a zahirance de babu abunda be hada ba,akwai kudi(born with a silver spoon),kyan fasali,qasaita,gayu,da ilimi~na boko da islama,du da cewan halayya da dabi'unsa sunso sui hannun riga da tarin ilimin dake tattare dashi,kangararre ma na ajin qarshe,
amman kash,babu zato babu tsammani,a cikin dare daya wani baqon lamari ya soma kunno masa,har abin ke neman taka muhimmiyar rawa gun dagula masa dukkan lissafi,comes from proudly muslim background,extremely rich nd influencial family~~~kamar yadda zahrah ta kasance dalibar data amsa sunanta,kama daga kan karatunta na islama har i zuwa na zamanin nan,sai ta zama jajirtacciya,sam bata wasa da ko wani dayansu,cikin tsari take bama dukkanin karatun da take haqqi,sam baza taso tai almazazzaranci da gumin iyayenta ba,kulawarsu da namijin qoqarin da suketa faman yi dan ganin sun gina rayuwar 'ya'yan da suka haifa bisa kan tafarkin dake cikeda inganci a tafe kan turba madaidaiciya,a yau Alhamis,da la'asariya sakaliyahar misalin 5:04pm na yamma,a ziyarar dana kai bakin makarantarnan ta ilimin kimiyya da fasaha,me taken Kano State Polytechnic (SOT),cincirundun dalibai na gani na kaiwa suna komowa bakin gate din makarantar,ko wanne soul na gwada yin harkokin dake gabansa cikin qasaita da jin kai,a sannu suka ringa fitowa,wasu na taran cab,wasu na trekking yayinda kuma wasu ke shiga tsadaddun motocin dake ta faman sintirin tsayawa daukansu,inanan de har sai da gun ya soma lafawa sai tsilla tsillan jama'a suka rage inda naketa raba idanu da niyyar yin tozali da wacca nakeson na bibiya,caraf na sauke idona a kan zahrah da qawarta Raheelah sun jero suna fitowa wajen gate din makaranta looking sophisticated,du ko da cewan kallo daya zakai musu ka tsinci tarin gajiya harma da yunwan daketa faman cinsu,zahrah farar halitta ce,a ciki da waje,doguwar fuskarta me sanye da annuri,dara daran idanunta,matsakaicin hancinta,da kyawawan labbanta,gata yar ficika kamar ka sace ka gudu,babu qiban babu tsawon,'yar firit da ita,dan dama daka ganta kaga typical bafulatana,
"girl,kema fa a karan kanki kinsan tunda muka kai har i yanxun skul dinnan mawuyaci ne samun mota nan gun ko,tun wuri ma,ki bar wahalar damu hk,gwamma mui trekking zuwa babban titi zefi mana,kinji",zahra ta fada cikin sautin murya me dauke da gajiya,both itan da Raheelah na ta yin iya bakin qoqarinsu na tsaida cab amman kowacca motar cike take,imma sunci sa'a an saurare sun se a yanke musu kudin daya wuce musu geji,
looking dissappointed raheelah ta gyara zaman handbag dintan dake saqale wuyanta tana jan tsaki,"wallahil~azeem kinji de rantsuwar musulmi nai miki,idan har Allah ya kaimu ranar da muka kammala qaddararran karatunnan,wallahi babu abinda ze hanani zuba ruwa qasa in sha",Raheelah ke fada cikin bacin rai,
hk suka ringa tafiya suna gwada tsaida mota yayinda ita zahrah takaicin da bata san dalilinsu duk suka bi suka dabaibayeta,bata iya fadin ko da uffan ne,se kunnuwantan daketa jin muzuran Raheelah,kamar daga sama suka ga durowan wasu matasa biyu gabansu,wanda kallo daya sukai musu suka gama aunen babu mutunci a tattare da su,duka sukai tsaye cirko cirko banda kallon kallo ba abinda kowannensu keyi,a taqaice dayan su ya nuna Zahra da yatsa,"ke juya ki biyo mu can,ana son ganinki",ya fada cikin isa da gadara sai kace wani ubanta,"bakada hnkl",raheelah ta fada cikin tsiwa tana binsu da harara a lkcnda ta figi hannun zahrah fuu sukai gaba,kamar daukewan ruwan sama hk naga zahrah ta tsaya cik,a dai dai lkcn ta miqama Raheelah tarin handouts din data riqe rungume a qirjinta,daga bisani,cikin wani irin yanayi tayi saurin juyowa tana jinjina irin wannan salo na iskanci,"yan iska,ku sake ni nace",ta fada cikeda masifa tana qoqarin fuzgan jelar hijabintan da suka kama suka riqe gam,"idan baso kike a keta miki haddi take a nan gun ba,so u keep it as simple as ki biyomu har can gun",dayansu ya fada a hnkl,trying to be calm yayinda yake mata nuna da can tsallake,bala'i,maganar da zahra taji ne kuma abinda ya kuma rikita mata dukkan lissafi,ai a haukace ta ringa kokuwar raba ruqon dasukai ma hijabinta da iya qarfin ta,amman ina qarfin mace bekai na maza ba,"Innalillahi
",abinda raheelah ta ringa fada cikin tashin hnkl dan ganin yadda suka feffella hijabin dake jikin zahrah to pieces,du da hkn zahra bata bar qoqarin da take dan qwatar kanta ba,tana qare su da zagi ta uwa ta uba,lkc guda naga dayansu yasa mata qafa ya kwasheta,tim,ta fadi nan take tana fashewa da kuka cikin ambaton Allah,cikin tashin hnkl Raheelah ta koma a sikwane zata tunkareta,daya cikin su yayo kanta gadan gadan yana dunqule hannunsa da niyyar kai mata naushi,"qara gaba nace,shegiya idan baso kike a nakasa ki yanxun ba",ya fada cikin kaushin murya yana baza mata jajayen idonsa,"idan kunai ma Allah ku tafican gun yan iskan mata irinku,dan Allah ku qyale ta,ku rabu damu,ku tafi,mu ba yan iskan mata bane,
",saukan naushin da taji bakinta ne yasa babu shiri ta datse zantukan ta,cikin rudani tasa hannu ta riqe bakin da yasoma fidda jini,hawaye na biyomata take kallon zahra da har yanxun bata samu daman dagowa ba banda kuka,tunanin halin da qawarta zata shiga take matsawar ta tafi ta barta da wa'annan mugayen,"akace ki kauce ko",dayansu ya daka mata tsawa yana kuma yowa kanta kamar ze doketa,a tsorace tai saurin yin baya,ta ringa baza ido gun da niyyar ko zasu samu mataimaki,amman cikin rashin sa'a,taga babu wasu isassun mutane dan lungun da suka biyo din ba idon jama'a bane,motocin ma dake biyowa hanyar tsilla tsilla ne,babu wanda kebi takansu,Raheelah ta hadiyi wani abu da qyar hawaye na kuma saukowa,dan sanin halin da muke ciki a yanxun da kowa harkar gabansa ya sani,sam mutane basu san taimako ba,ganin batada wani alternative yasa ta soma tfy kamar kazar da qwai ya fashema a ciki,sai waigowa take tana ganin yadda zahrah ke ta faman tirje musu tana qoqarin qwatar kanta ga ruqon da sukai mata,"mugaye kawai,wlh Allah sai ya saka miki,in sha Allah baze bari su idda mummunan qudurinsu ba",Raheelah ta fada cikin kuka tana jan majina,
"kai,wa'anne 'yan bantan uban ne nan",sautin muryan da akeji na tunkarowa gun knn,da saurin gaske dukkaninsu suka juya gun da ake jiyo muryan dan ganin ko su waye,wasu police ne su su biyu suna nufan gun da dogayen sandunan su a hannu,wani dariyan jindadi Raheelah tai tana hamdala,"wallahi su ne yan iskan,iskanci suke son sui mata",a sittin matasan nan suka saki zahra,kafin kace me ai tuni ko wanne dan iskan ya sanyama wandonsa iska,
tofa,u keep on following me woooo,dan kuga yadda zanta muku unveiling every piece of d story dat have been a fortunate dream come true,

ZUCIYAR MUTUM BIRNINSA - 2~So Sanadi - Page 2 - Wattpad
ZUCIYAR MUTUM BIRNINSAWhat a freaking love story,UmmySaudah
Saudat Adam Isah2
A yau din daya kasance Litinin misalin qarfe 12 dai dai na Rana,
cikin ziyarar dana kai Kanopoly(SOT),a department dinnan na SLT(science laboratory technology),dalibai ne a ko ta ina maqil na tsaka da yin harkokin dake gabansu,a can na hangi zahra cikin casual look dinta na baqar Abaya,harda sauran 'yan gang dinta zaune kan concrete seats irin wanda aka tanadar dan zaman dalibai,a daidai gindin wata qatuwar bishiyar cashew inda suka baje koli,dangin littafai,irinsu pamphlets,manuals,graphs,plainsheets din dake gabansu basa qirguwa,a lkcnda ko wannensu ya tattare dukkanin hnklnsa ya aza akan aikin dake gabansa se naga zahra ta fita zakkah,dan da ace zaka lura da itan se kai ta faman qirga tsakin da taketa jerawa babu iyaka,at thesame time kana ganinta kagama sanin zurfin datai cikin duniyar tunani ba dan qanqani bane,sai can naga ta sauke hannun tagumin tana qoqarin maida qwallan daya cika mata ido,"Allah ya isa na",ta fada a kan lebenta tana kuma buga wani tsakin,ranta duk a dagule tasa hannu ta wafci wata takaddar dake gefen hagunta,a dai dai lkcn ta kifa kanta tana kwashe rubutun dake kan takardar a cikin record book,bata dauki wani lkc me tsawo ba ta dago tana kallon wadda ke kusa da ita me suna yusrah,"babe,gashinan an kammala yin recording,sauran ki qarashe drawing din,idan dakwai wasu ideas din sai ku qara kafin ai submitting",zahra tai zancen tana ajje record book din kan cinyan yusrah,daga bisani ta miqe tsaye tana tattare tarkacenta gu daya,sai a sannan yusrah'n ta dago daga duban da take ma ipad din hannunta tana maida kallonta ga zahra,a cikeda tuhuma ba tareda tayi magana ba,hkn yasa zahra wara mata manyan idanunta masu haske,"nd whats with dat look",ta fada tana rufe murfin biron dake hannunta,"malama ina zuwa kuma",yusrah ta tmbyta,"where else banda gidan ubana",zahra ta bata amsa tana murmushin yaqen da be kai ko maqogaro ba,dan takaici da baqincikin da take na skipping lectures din da zatai ba dan qarami bane,kawai dan batada wani choice din me sauki bayan wannan shys,sanin ko ya take qaunar karatun,lafiya da kwanciyar hnklnta ne a gaba,cikin rashin gamsuwa yusra ta cabe baki tana fadin,"u re not serious right,tunda kema kinsan yanxunnan zamu shiga heat energy(STP112),kuma a bayanshi ga electronic logic for science(STP114)",cikin wani yanayi zahra ta tabe dan qaramin baqinta,da fuska ba alamun wasa tace,"wallahi Allah da gaske nake,masifaffen ciwon ciki ya bi ya addabeni,gwamma na tafi gidan shine zefi",tai qarya coz d real fact din shine tsoron karta doshi yammaci bata fita skull din bane,dan sam baza taso abinda ya faru da ita rannan sake maimaita kansa ba,bugu da qari gashi yau raheelah bata zo ba,kuma gashi cikin tarin qawayentan da suka hada department daya daga ita din se raheelah ne suka hada hanya guda,se a sannan wacca ke kusa da yusrah me suna zainab da namijin dake dab da ita wato ammar suka tsoma bakkuna sunai mata Allah ya sauwaqe,ita zainab cikin raha da daga murya ta cigaba da fadin,"amman fa wannan ciwon cikin naki qunqume ne kam,tunda har ya saki breaking golden record",yusrah tai saurin amshewa,"for d first time in history,d whole sensational genius in our pot,d whole miss Mukhtar naAllah wan skip lectures today wo",ta qare zancen cikin dariya suna cafkewa da zainab,"banni da lkcn sauraron haukan mahaukata de",zahrah ta fada a cikeda jin haushin su ta juya tana tfy kamar bata son yi,ai kamar ana tunzurasu naga sun kuma kwashewa da wata gagarumar dariyan,"ai da sauqi tunda jirgi daya ya kwasomu duka,kinga knn ke dimma a cikin jerin mahaukatan kike",inji zainab tana kuma fashewa da dariya,"kanku akeji fa",zahra dake tafe ta fada cikin sautin muryan datasan zasu jiyo,"Twinkle,ki rabu dasu de kinji,inanan anan gun zan rama miki ne",cewar ammar cikin daga murya,daidai lkcn kamar wacca ta tuna abu zahra tai saurin juyawa tana kallon ammar take fadin,"yauwa ammar zo ka rakani bakin gate dan Allah",
suna tsaye bakin makarantar har seda ammar ya tsare ma zahrah mota sannan ya juya,
tun shigar zahra cikin motan take ta jin yadda gabanta ke faduwa,babban abinda ya daure mata kai shine dalilin da ya sa har ta hau taxi,se kace aikin rufa ido,dan a tsawon one year plus din datai a poly bata taba ganin taxi ya biyo ta gaban makarantar su ba,bata taba hawa taxi ba,tana tsaka da wannan tunanin se gani tai ana zuge ilahirin glasses din motan,dai dai lkcn aka figi motan da gudun gaske aka yanke hanya ba hanyar data saba biyowa ba,hkn ya kuma tabbatar mata kan cewan ba lfy ba,a lkc guda tabi ta tsure,hnklnta idan yayi dubu ya tashi,ta dingi buga tint glass din motan da qarfi,cikin kuka murya a sarqe ta soma fadin,"bawan Allah,me kake nufi ne,ya naga ka biyo dani tanan gun bayan munyi da kai unguwar kundila zaka kaini",ta glass din motan sukai ido hudu da Najib,"wow",shine impression din daya hau kaina a daidai lkcn dana sauke idona kansa,na bishi da kallon qurilla me kyau,wani irin kyau yake dashi wanda ke da wuyan lissafi,fuskarsa zaka kalla amman se kai ta faman qirga abubuwa da dama,irin mazajennan ne fitattu wa'anda suka amsa sunansu,wato ina nufin me cikakken qira da fasali,du da cewan a zaune yake be hanani gane cewan shi Dogo ne ba,da faffafan qirjinsa wanda yake bayyanar da 6-packs din shi saboda tsabar workout,ba fari bane kuma ba za'a sashi cikin sahun baqaqe irin baqiqqirin dinnan ba,kalar fatarsa me kyau irin kamar umber chocolate,yana da dogon hanci wanda ya dace da kyawawan pink lips din shi,gashin kanshi luf luf a kwance har ya gangaro izuwa well groomed sajensa saboda tsaban gyaran da yake sha,
wani malalacin murmushi ya sakar mata yana kashe mata idonsa daya kana ya tamke fuska,"shshshshsh",ya fada a hnkl hannunsa kan lips dinsa,sannan ya maida kansa ga titi inda ya cigaba da falfala uban gudu kamar ance masa 'run or die',hkn ya haddasa ma zahra wani irin shock din daya sata yin still na tsawon lkc,daga bisani tai zumbur,a dai dai lkcn wani marayan kuka ya qufce mata,ihu ta ringa yi tana kallon waje cikin neman doki amman ina,babu wanda ke ganinta bare ya ji ta,ta ringa qoqarin balle murfin motan da iya qarfin da ya rage mata amman ina tuni najib ya qulle qofar ta ciki,"innalillahi
,wayyo Allah,ka tsaya dan Allah",ta kuma fada cikin tashin hnkl tana bubbuga ko ina na motan kamar batasan ciwon jikinta ba,a lkc guda ta gama susucewa cikin fitar hayyaci kamar ba ita ba,banda ihun kukan da take ba abinda ya cikama Najib kunne,har cikin qwaqwalwarsa yakejin kidan kamar bugun guduma,abun duniyan ya bi ya isheshi ba kadan ba,hkn yasa besan a lkcnda ya samu gefe guda yai parking ba,ya dafa kai cikin yanayinsa me wuyar misali karan kansa na mamakin kansa coz dis is totally unlike him,ya saba jin kuka da kuwar mata amman sam basu tabai masa tasiri kamar nata ba,"lock up d damn mouth dan uwarki",ya fada cikin tsawan dayasa yan hanjin cikin zarah kadawa,ta kame kanta gu daya jikinta na qyarma,amman taurin kanta be sata yin shiru kamar yadda ya fada ba,"anqi ai shirun,shege mugu azzalumi kawai,nd uwarka ka zaga,bade uwata ba wallahi",ta fada cikin tsiwa tana cigaba da buga seat din da yake,hkn ya kuma harziqa shi,lkc guda yasa hannu ya lalubo bindigar dake cikin pocket din jeans pant dinsa,ya yunquro cikin zafin nama ya cafko hannunta yana murdawa a cikeda mugunta,banda ihun azaba ba abinda zahrah ta cigaba dayi tana jan numfashi a wahalce kamar zata shide,har se da ya kusa karya mata qashi ya sake mata hannu ya tunkudata baya,banda huci ba abinda yake yana fiffito da qwala qwalan idonsan da tuni suka cika da qwalla tsabagen masifa,ya nunata da bindigar,"just one word from u,nd i wont think twice of messing up d fucking brain of urs,yaseen babu abinda ze hana in fasa miki kai take a nan gun,just dare me nd see,wawiya,qaramar mara kunya kawai",ya fada cikin kaushin murya sai kallon yadda zarah ta tattare kanta gu daya yake cikeda tsoronsa tana rawan sanyi,yayinda gumi ya gama wanke mata jiki,ya ringa bin taqaitaccen image dinta da kallo yanajin wani baqon abu na tsirga masa zuciya,be san dalilin dayasa yaketa jin wani irin extraordinary feeling hk gameda ita ba,ko ma menene yasan ba sha'awa bane,dan baya tunanin dakwai kalar macen dabe dandani zumar ta yasan irinta a ciki da waje ba,amman se wannan ta fita daban dasu,yake mamakin dalilin daya sa tun daga ranar dayai tozali da itan,ta shiga rayuwarsa tai masa gagarumin tasiri hk,ya zama idan be samu daman ganinta ba yake dai dai da rasa duk wani sukuni na rayuwarsa,cikin wani yanayi ya ringa tona chewing gum din bakinsa yana kafeta da ido kamar a yau ya soma ganin mace,a sannu a hnkl baqar zuciyarsa ta ringa kitsa masa mugayen quduri kan zahra,dai dai lkcn ya fuzar da chewing gum din dake bakinsa ya sauka a kan fuskar zahra,hkn yasata yin firgigit ta kuma matse kanta a cikeda firgici,tana kafeshi da idanun da keta fidda hawaye sharr kamar fanfo,kamar masquerade hk take ta kallonsa dan kama i yanxun sosai tsoronsa ya gama shigarta,du da yadda takeson ta qwaci kanta amman hk nerves dinta sukai dissappointing dinta,ta gaza tabuka komai se addu'oin da take tayi cikin rawar baki,yana cikin kallon innocent nd cute face dinta har wani shu'umin murmushi ya bayyana gefen fuskarsa,wanda kana gani ka gama aunen na mugunta ne,babu ko 'dugon tausayinta a ransa dan ko akwai din a yanxun mugun hasashen da zuciyarsa ke ta hasko masa se ya bi ya disashe uban komai,"atlast,se gashi yau yarinya ta shigo hannun maza",ya fada yana lashe lips dinsa a lkcnda ya zuge seat din da yake kai qasa,yai wani shegen tsalle ya duri baya,ya matso ya matse jikinsa dana zahrah,
kar ku bari a baku labari,u just keep on going,dan ganin qarshen wannan kwamacalan,harma da wa'anda ke shirin zuwa gaba,

ZUCIYAR MUTUM BIRNINSA - 3~Tun a ranar - Page 2 - Wattpad
ZUCIYAR MUTUM BIRNINSAWhat a freaking love story
By UmmySaudahSaudat Adam Isah
3~
wani marayan kuka ne ya qufce ma zahra,a daidai lkcn tai saurin hada kai da guiwa,tana kuma matse jikinta da bangon motan,
"matsayinka na musulmi,nakeson ka dubi girman Allah,ka dubi soyayyar da kakema manzonSa,ka auna skelin su,ka rabu dani kaji,kada ka cutar dani,ka tuna azabar da Allah ya tanadar dan azzaluman bayi,dan Allah ka qyaleni in tafi",
ta ringa fada cikin kuka tana kuma dunqule kanta gu daya,abun de gwanin ban tausayi,
"shshsh,yimin shiru nan banson hayaniya dalla,ko a zaton da kike wa'annan surutannaki na banza da hofi sun isa har su sauya min tunani ne,
pause yai yana jan tsaki a lkcnda ya cillar da bindigar dake hannunsa,for d second time ya kuma sa hannunsa cikin aljihu,this time around se ganinsa nai ya lalubo protective ya ajje shi nan gefe,yana kuma goga jikinsa da nata,kuma a dai dai lkcn yake kallon ko ina na motan,a cikeda takaici ya kuma auna wani tsakin,wai yau har shine yai downgrading kansa up to dis degree,shine cikin irin kalan motan nan,duk wai sbd wannan 'yar yarinyar,yai zancen da zuciyarsa yana kuma qare mata kallo,
cikin wannan lkcn baki bude da mamaki kamar ze kashesa yake cigaba da kallon irin wannan iko na Allah,dan a zamaninnan de besan da cewan akwai 'yan'mata irin zahra ba,
"wai meye a cikine,me da zaki bi har ki ringa azabtar da kanki haka,abu me dadi zami fa,sounding as simple as d two of us fucking each others ass,it's all safe,babu ruwanki da wata damuwa,so dan hk tun wuri nakeson ki gaggauta bani hadin kai mu fara abinda zami mu qareshi yanxun cikin jindadi,idan baso kike nai miki ta qarfi da yaji ba,nd bayan na gama iskancin danake son yi in kasheki take in kashe banza",

an dauki tsawon lkc a hk yayinda ko wannensu keda agenda'n da yake ta faman saqawa cikin rai,
bangaren zahrah takejin kanta kamar ta hadiyi rai ta mutu,a karon farko knn da wani gardin can da ba muharraminta ya taba jikinta,"Allah ya isa na,dan iska,shege,dan akuya kawai",ta ringa kwashe masa albarka cikin kukan zuci,jin shirun yayi yawa yasata tsagaita abinda take,ta gefen ido ta seta kallon gefenta,take idanun suka diri cikin na najib,ya sakar mata wani kalan qayataccen murmushinsa me tsayawa a rai,wani irin feeling din da taji ne yasa tai saurin dauke kanta gefe zuciyarta na harbawa cikeda tsanan sa a cakude har ma da tsoron,yayinda wata zuciyar ta kafe ta ringa tariyo mata fuskarsa din tana yaba irin kyawunsa,"me kyan dan maciji knn,mugu,azzalumin bawa",

',ai abinda ya taimaka gun ingiza tashin hnkln Dr mukhtar da Saudah knn,wato mahaifan zahra,a ranar suka kasa tsaye suka kasa zaune,sune har kafafan watsa labarai cigiyarta,har se washe gari suka samu labarin gun da take,amman babu inda suka tsinkayi babban abun al'ajabi se a lkcnda suka ga irin yadda aka keta ma yar qaramar 'yarsu mutuncinta,aka lalata mata rayuwa ta hanyar fyade,tsinuwa da Allah ya isa kam babu irin wanda basui ba,gutsuri tsoman mutanen unguwa yasa sukai qaura daga unguwar da suke suka dawo nan Kundila inda a lkcn ginin dake gun dai dai kune~

6
it's exactly a week after,nd like expected,things keeps on revolving d way they reckon to be,
on a faithful saturday afternoon,qarfe 12 na rana da yan tsirarun mintina,can gindin qofa na gano zahrah ta bullo kaman yanda na ga sauran dalibai ke firfitowa,fitowansu knn sun kammala test din da suka halarta cikin theatre hall din SGS,jikinta lullube da zulmemen hijabi me kalan dorawa wanda be bani daman ganin ko da suturar dake lafe qarqashin jikinta ba,banda takalmin dake manne qafanta din na Vine kalarsa black,me shegen tudu,dan daman akwai aukin saka su,ko badan komai ba din,ohh fairly to boost her confidence,kafadanta a saqale da handbag dinta na Valentino,a yanayin da take yanxun ba kamar sati biyu baya ba,sabili ga yadda tayi sanyi sosai cikin lamuranta dan kallo daya zakai mata din ka fayyace ma kanka hkn
"ya salam",
ta fada qasan lebenta cikin daburcewa a lkcnda qiris ya rage mata kifewa qasa a sanadin tuntuben da qafanta yai,a kasalance tai qoqarin regaining balance tana baza ido da niyyan samun gun rakubewa,a sannu ta samu gu can ta takure inda ma tasan su raheelah basu isa sun ga wani trace dinta ba,dan kama i yanxun sune mutane na qarshe da zatai mararin sawa a idonta,ta jingina da bangon dake gun hadi da lumshe idanu,tunanin dake neman kawo mata farmaqi yasa ta saurin bude idanun tana jan numfashi,trying to get rid of tragic feelings yasa har ta sa hannu ta lalubo essentials dinta cikin handbag da niyyan qarasa pending work din da zatai submitting a yau,tuni tai nisa har ta idda,nd dat works coz nothing distressing popped in,se taji dadin gun,so pacific,babu hayaniyan su raheelah,their pestering nature nd all,
dayan aikin wanda zata hada tai submitting take nema cikin jakan amman yace daukenni inda kika ajjeni,qarshe wayanta me qirar tecno K7,ta dauko ta shiga dialing layin khairat,bugu daya zuwa na biyu aka dauka,"kina ina ne",
"ya akai,ina gida mana",khairat ta amsata,
"maza jeki dakina ki lalubomin graph note dina na mechanics(STP111),ki duba dan bazan iya ce miki ga gun da yake ba,kawomin skul yanxunnan zanyi submitting",tana kaiwa nan ta katse kiran dan sarai tasan khairat se ta nemi musanta mata,she could have spared d fuss,dan kawai yau ne deadline,ata dalilin monday zasu fara exams,gashi komai nata se slow yake tayi,wanda ya samo asali musabbabin fashin da tai kwanakin baya,bugu da qari Anxiety wanda ya tilasta mata rashin maida kai,a kaikaice ta dauko madubin dake cikin bag dinta,ta qura ma fuskanta ido tana kallon yadda tai wani qayau qayau da ita,sosai fuskanta ya fa'da,kai barimma ace idanun da suka wani qwalalo kamar zasi magana,"ya Allah,am not my self,Agajin Ka",ta fada ma kanta with so much dissappointment tana tattare kayanta,daga hk ta miqe ta nufi SOT,ganin wayam babu kowa inda course mates dinta suka saba zaman dirshan,yasa ta duba time 1:25pm,se da ta tafi common room ta sauke farali,da qyar ta iya tura cupcake din data saya,dan maganin yunwa bawai dan jindadin bakinta ba,dan kamar yadda take jin kanta yanxun gaba daya lamuran duniya sun fitar mata ka,babu wani abinda take yi dan jindadin kanta se wanda ya zame mata kamar dole,nan ta zarce block 5,Venue din next lecture dinsu na 1to3,
ana fitowa lectures ta kuma samun gefe guda ta ke'be banda haqurin jiran zuwan khairat ba abinda take tayi,jin an dafa ta ta baya ne yasata yin zumbur ta juya kanta,ganin raheelah yasata hade rai ta juyar da kai tana jan siririn tsaki,tafa hannaye raheelah ta hau yi dan ganin look din dake kan fuskan aminiyar ta ta,"wonders shall never end,besty ni din,ni kikema kallon kitse",tai zancen in a funny way pretending like nothing happened earlier,murmusawa tai tana zama dab da zahra,hadi da zagaye hannunta wuyanta,"haba besty ta ta kaina,wai meye yai zafi hk,karki so ganin yadda su yusra ketamin dariya mana,wai sun gammu cikin rana",raheelah ta fada cikin raha tana kallon fuskan zahrah,ganin babu ko 'dugon annuri kai ne yasata maida abin da gaske,ta 'dora,"yes,i was'nt thinking straight,nd i recognized afterwards dat i could'nt have told them like dat,buh i apologise,nd am sorry,tashi mu tafi gida da Allah,komai ya wuce kinji qawa,ki bar damuwa Allah ze musanya miki wanda yafi jabir",raheelah ta fada har cikin zuciyanta,amman du da wannan bata burge zahra ba,hk zahra tai wani funfurufus da ita kamar batasan da ajiyar mutum gun ba,ka'da kai raheelah ta dingi yi,"taa hau dokin zuciyan nata knn,kuma lalle bata shirya saukowa ba",ta ra'da a rai,har hkn yabata daman cigaba da fadin abinda ke cikinta,
"just take a look at ur self,kinanan kina neman ki 'bata wayonki a kan wani can da be damu da sabgarki ba,tun wuri ma ki miqe ki maida hnkl gun samar ma kanki wanda ya fishi,shi kuma duniya ce a sannu zai gane kuskuren dayai na rabuwa da kyakyawan mace irin ki,kuma ba akanki aka fara fasa aure ba,da har dan na fada ma wasu zaki tsiri Gaba dani,nd banda salon qauyancin ki ma meye abin boyewa ciki,fadamin ya za ai ki cigaba da boye abinda fitowarsa is for ur own ease,bayan kowa a tunaninsa din u're counting on days to ur wedding,would'nt dat hurt u more,Hello",raheelah ta fada sounding frank,cikin salon tsokana take qoqarin zaran littafin dake cikin hannun zahra,se a sannan zahra ta daga kai ta kalleta,dede tsakiyan qirjinta na bugawa a cikeda takaicin irin cin fuskan raheelah du da tasan dakwai gsky cikin kalamanta amman haushintan da take ji a lkcn ya danne wannan,a qufule tasa hannu ta ture hannunta,"dalla malama kin isheni,nd just looking at ur face makes me sick,dan hk ni ki ficemin ido,am fed up with ur presence,qara gaba",ta qare zancen cikeda bala'i yayinda lamura suka tsiri dawo mata sabo,raheelah ta miqe a taqaice ta barta nan nata faman cika tana batsewa,dai de lkcn kuma qoqarin maida qwallan dake barazanan cika mata ido take,wanda tarin ALHININ dake maqil a ranta ya taimaka gun bankadosa,tana kuma tariyo hoton abinda raheelah tai mata,how humiliated she feels dazun da ake fada ma mutane wai an soke bikinta har suka maida abin topic of discussion,how embarassing,
har take gode ma Allah dayasa batai gangancin fadamata main issue'n daya raba ta da jabir ba,da hk zata zo ta kwance mata zani a kasuwa a karan babu gaira babu dalili,a hk har ta zarce ta cigaba da karanta wasiqar jaki,tanajin kanta kaman bata cancanci uban komai ba ma,bata da hurumin da wai zata bugi qirji tana me ambaton cewan ita 'budurwace',ta riga data rasa wannan,itadin ba abar alfahari bace,gun mijin da zata aura gaba baze kasance me alfahari da ita ba,ba kaman sauran 'yammatan da suka amsa sunansu ba,suka shigo da 'yammatancin har a cikin turakan mazajen da aka aura musu,de de lkcn da ta tuna da sakayyar Ubangijinta,se ta dan ji sanyi,dakwai wani abin dayai mata karan tsaye a ranta,shine,ko kadan mesa cin zarafin da aka mata bei tab'a mata ryw ba,deda rana d'aya bata tab'a tunawa da komai ba,even a single shot,mesa,mesa se a bakin umma take jin labarin dayai mata kama da tsatsuniya,kamar bada ita faruwan hkn ta kasance ba,kacal,shekarunta a duniya hud'u a lkcn,sabida meye,sbd kuruciyako yaronta,ta tmby kanta,dan ta girma tanajin labarai kala iri iri gameda qananan yaran da akai molesting ta hanyar fyade,wannan yakan taka masu muhimmiyar rawa a gun assasa masu juyayi a ryw,cutar tsoro,damuwa,zullumi da firgici irinsu,depression,anxiety,trauma,psychopathy,ko lalacewar tarbiyyarsu,makamantan wa'annan duka basu shafeta ba,Alhamdulillahda wannan zahra ta kuma jin wani d'ugo na sanyi naa tsirga tsakiyar qirjinta,yana sanyata godiya ga Allah Akbar,me girman ikon dayai mata wannan gatan,gatan da baa ko wani mahaluqi ne ke dacewa da irinsa ba,
har ta ida tunane tunanenta ta dawo ga mamakinta taga khairat a kanta,dariya khairat din keyi tana qarema zahra kallo,"lalle Yaya,kinganki kuwa,how Weired,wlh kamar wacca aka koro",take fada dan har ga Allah ma bata fuskanci hk yayartasu ta dawo ba se yanxun,cikin tsarguwa zahra ke kallon kanta from head to toe,"ya nake da Allah",ta tmbyi khairat a sanyaye,khairat ta cigaba da kallonta tana 'dan dariya bata samu daman bata amsa ba,ganin abinnata wulaqanci ne yasata 'dan ture kafadanta,"ke banson raini",ta fada cikin tsiwa tana jan tsaki,a fusace ta wafci littafin dake hannun khairat,takai tai submitting kamin sukai hanyar fita~
~
kaman yadda yin hkn ya zame masa tamkar ibada a hk ya kasance a kullum kamin ya wuce gun aiki ko idan ya taso daga aikin,gaban makarantan ya zama hanyar binsa,buqatarshi a kullum be wuce yai tozali da kyakkyawan halittar da ko kadan ganinta be taba gajiyar dashi,kamar kullum can a gefen titin da ke fuskantan gaban makarantan SOT ya paka motansa me qiran Mercedes-AMG Project One kalarsa blueblack,cikin shigarsa ta qasaitattun matasan dake taqama da zallan quruciyarsu,gayu da aji,banda tashin qamshi da sanyin AC ba abinda akeji na tsirgawa,daga cikin tinct shade din motan ya seta idanunsa tsaye bakin gate din,da kaf hnklnsa ya miqa kaman dan yai hakan aka halittosa,
da kallon qurilla yaketa lura da kowanne dalibin dake fitowa,cikin sa'a se ga idonsa kan siffar da tafi uban komai sanya masa nutsuwa da annashuwa a rayuwa,du da cewan besan dalili ba amman abinda ya sani shine itadin ta daban ce,sosai ta zame masa fitacciya cikin tarin abokan karatun natan dake gun a yanxu,kai har dama sauran mata gaba daya,

nd i've never been this sure,am so so deeply in love with her",ya ringa sumbatu kaman wani zautacce,dubansa na kanta ya cigaba da ayyanata da lamura masu fadin gaske,har se da yaji 'dandanon abin nasa na neman motsawa,ya dauke idonsa a kanta yana cije lebe,cikin himma ya tada motan yaja a sannu yake nufan gun dasu zahra ke tsaye suna taran cab,

zahra,data gaza miqe tsayinta duka,wasu 'yammatu biyu da khairat suka daddafata,kafaffun hawaye ne kawai keta mata ambaliya a fuska,fuskan da tuni yai wani jazur ya fita hayyacinsa,gaban goshintan shirya qauqautawa,"zahra",ya fada a sanyaye a lkcnda yai qoqarin daga qafafunsa na nufan gun da take,wani irin zumbur tai cikin kidima,tasa ihu tana kuma shishshigewa jikin jama'an dake gun,"da Allah ku taimaka ku 'boyeni,wlh ni tsoronsa nake",ta iya fada a wahalce tana wuwwurga ido tsakanin jama'an dake gun da najib,jin tsakankanin qirjinsa yai na neman darewa tsaban takaici,hkn yasashi juyawa gun a taqaice ya tafi cikin motansa,zafafan hawaye suka soma biyowa kuncinsa,yadda yake jin kansa a yanxun kaman yaje ya shaqe mufida ta mutu mus har lahira,hakanan tun kamin ya faro gini har ta rushe masa komai,idanunsa tsaye gun har aka taran ma su zahra keke napep suka tafi,cikin tunanin yanxun har yaushe ze samu sauqin abinda yake ji,taya za ai ya samu daman dandana soyayyar da zuciyarsa ke muradin samu daga gunta,yanaso ya gyara abinda ya faru tsakaninsa da ita baya ga wani nan ya hada masa goma da ashirin,idonsa naa gun mufida har yaga ta miqe a galabaice,dede lkcn yasa kai ya fita a hargitse, har gun da take ya je ya fixgo hannunta,fuu ya jata suka shiga motanta ya ja murfin ya rufe shi gam,babu 'bata lokaci ya soma gwada abinda zuciyarsa ta ayyana masa,wuyanta ya shaqe da qarfin da ya sa har ta soma jin qamshin barzahu,har se da numfashi ya soma barin jikinta sannan ya saketa,taa wani tsure,idanun sukai 'bula 'bula da ilahirin jijiyoyin jikinta,ta riqe wuyan tana tari a wahalce,cikin tashin hnkl take kallon sa da niyyan yin magana amman tarin yaqi sakinta,"nd am not done with u yet,
kika kuma yin gigin ko da kallon yarinyar nan ne,yaseen wlh se kin 'dandana ma aya zaqinta,se na gwada miki asalin kalana,wanda baza ki ta'ba tsammanin ni din ke dashi ba,u mark my word",ya fada cikin hucin masifa hadi da fita ya banko murfin motan da mugun qarfi,batare da ya tsaya kallon taron jama'an dake gun ba ya shige mota ya ja da mahaukacin gudu kaman wanda ke shirin tashi sama~
~
har se bayan magrib su zahrah suka isa gida,wani abu ta ringa ji gameda najib wanda batasan ya misalinsa yake ba,tanason tai kuka a lkcn ko dan taji sauqin abinda ke damunta amman se taga idonta ya bushe tunanin abinda ya faru ne kawai keta mata yawo aka,hk zalika zuciyarta a cunkushe take tunanin meye ya hassaso faruwan hkn,kurarin da mufida ta ringa yi da zantuka ta ringa jujjuyawa,qarshe ta nemi kauda tunanin har ta sauke idonta kan khairat data kafeta da mayun idanu tanai mata kallon tuhuma,"Yaya fadamin meye ya faru dazun,wacece wancar ,waye wannan",khairat ta jera mata tmbyy,murtuk zahra tai ta hade rai,"a word of advice,wlh,tallahi,kika kuskura kika fadama umma,even a tiny word a kaina da duk wani abun relating to this,i promise,u will have to deal with me,and that's a warning,aikin banza,bigmouth kawai",qare zancen tai tana jan wani shegen tsaki hadi da watsama khairat harara kamar idanun su zazzago dan tasan idan ba hkn tai mata ba din komai a kunnen umma,
tabe baki khairat tai kawai ta fice a sanyaye tana qunquni,
se da zahra ta je ta gabatar da sallah'n magrib wanda da qyar take jure yin sujjada sbd ciwon dake goshinta,tai azkar hadi da karanta Suratul~Rahman sannan ta danji zuciyanta ya lafa,taje tai dressing ciwon dake goshinta,hijabin data cire dazun ta kalla tana kuma jin takaicin abinda ya faru dazun,ga yadda take jin jikinta yayi tsami saboda gwabzan data sha a hannun mufida,amman a dede lkcnda tunanin najib ya gifta mata se taji sanyi na ratsa qirjinta,wanda karan kanta na mamakin kanta,da hk ta samu ta dauko wani zulmemen hijabin ta zulma hadi da rufe goshin yadda umma bazata fuskanci komai ba,ta dan gyara idontan daya wani kumburo ya canza launi da taimakon cometics,tai gathering courage,sannan ta yunqura ta shige dakin umma,

idda tarkata lamuranta kaf dinsu ta jingine a ha'de da fawwala ma Allah,Al Hakeemu,du ko da cewan cikin lamura da dama she just cant help it,dan tun both incidents din da sukai diran mikiya a gareta(batun fyaden da soke bikintan da akayi),shine suka hadu suka ringa yin fure har suka sanyata aza karan tsana ta 'dora a kan ilahirin bainan ahalin Matasan dasuka amsa sunan NAMIJI,bataso ta tsaya ko inuwa daya ne a ra'be dasu,bata tsayawa saurarensu bare har wata alaqa ta shiga tsakaninsu,bayan data idda zurfafa tunani a gun kafa hujjojin cewan babu wata rayuwa me tattare da dadin dayai mata saura daga yanzun har illa Masha Allah,tunda a yadda lissafinta yake shine daman duk wani farinciki,'yanci,qasaita da tunqahon duk wata 'ya mace a duniyarta be wuce a dakin mijinta,kuma sosai ta riga data idda haqiqancema kan ta cewan ta riga data rasa wannan,ta kuma yin zurfi da lissafa kyakkyawan soyayyan da tai da jabeer,irin son da suka ringa gwada ma junansu,ko a badini bata taba zargin wai dakwai wani abun da ze sanyashi gudunta ba,she hate to think dat way buh is d damn fact she must accept,tasan ko waye ya kuma fitowa hk ze mata,tabbas tasan da zaran labarinta ya iso kunnuwansa shima da hk ze gujeta,basu tunanin cewan ita victim ce,bazasu tausayama lamarinta ba,idanunsu a rufe se son zuciyarsu,da hk ne ta ringa daukar ma kanta alwashin cewan babu dalilin daze sanyata kuma sauraron wani 'da namiji,bazata kuma gigin bude ma wani dan' iskan qofan da har ze sa ya kuma bata wani heartbreak din ba,ta tsani maza,ta la'anci gaba daya clan dinsu,babu imani da tausayi a 1 yabi ya addabi hancina,lissafina be idda hargitsewa ba har se a cikin daqiqun da nai katarin ganin bullowan qerarren gangan jikinsa dungurungum,wani kalan azababben kyau yai de gwanin ban sha'awa,saman kyakkyawan fuskarsa ke fidda salon annuri na daban,me tattare da asalin kwarjinin da ban taba aunen yana dashi ba,murmurarren jikinsa na sanye da wani sabon salon shigar gezna caftan din daya fita daban dana saura,irin code din shigan ainihin matashin da ya gaji da sanin zamani,meji da asalin gayu,qwalisa da kuma uwar kudi,wata hadaddiyar hula a kife saman lallausan baqar suman kansa wanda ya zauna masa daram kuma ya hau da salon shigarsa,a zagaye wrist dinsa tsadadden agogo ne me kyau da tsada na blancpain le brassus,qafafunsa rufe da sau cikin takalminsa na Santoni,wanda ya kuma qawata cikar gayunsa,ya samu ya jingine da jikin motansa,iPhone XS da galaxy note 9 har da keys din dake hannunsa ya jefasu cikin aljihu,a nan ne har ya samu daman hada hannayensa biyu ya rungumesu saman qirjinsa,dubansa na fuskantan setin 'dan qaramin mashigar gate din gidan,wai shinenan yau har da tattaki ya biyo yarinya gidan ubanta,d traditional way fa,da zumman aure,which is so so unlike him,lalle,haqiqa Allah ya cancanci a gode masa,Alhamdulillah,Allah qara ma Annabi daraja,daga nanne har ya zarce da tunani kala iri iri,can na kafe da karantan ainihin fargaban dake kunno masa take,wanda har yake neman ya dunkufar da zumudin farincikin da yake ciki,"no no,'m always a winner,'m irresistible ai,i swear wlh nasan she must give in,sei tai soni",ya ringa yin iya qoqarinsa don ganin ya kore ma kansa batun da ke tafe da cewan bazatai na'am dashi ba,dan all his life be yarda da wani feeling na babu ba,be taba son wani abu bei sameshi ba,ko yaya abin yake,ballantana kuma zahra,wadda ta riga data disashe uban kowa da komai,his top aspiration

Najib kansa na qasa be iya fadin ko da uffan ba,daga shi se Allah suka san matsalolin dake farautan tunaninsa a halin yanzun,deda cewan Malam iliyasu irin hatsabibun mutanennan ne,duk kuwa da cewan sam sam shi be son ya kauce hanya,da ayoyin Allah yake bin lamuransa,sede ya kasance ire iren wa'anda rufanai ke hawa kansu,har a yanzun ma mutanen nasa basui qasa a guiwa ba,suka karance masa ainihin batutuwan dake addaban tunanin Najib a halin yanzun,ya kafe yanai masa duban tsanaki,a sannan ne ya jinjina kansa da fadin,"batun mahaifiyarka,addu'a tafi buqata daga gareka,ka qaddaraa kwanakintane suka qare a duniya,tunanin da kake tayi a kan cewan kai ne nan kai silan rasuwanta sam bazasu taimakeka ba,kade yi haquri kai tawassali faruwan komai duk a hannun Allah suke,duka da gamuwanka da wa'annan miyagun mutanen ba yin kanka bane,kuma kada ka samu damuwa,zami maka iyaka dasu,Allah yaa fisu,ayau dinnan dede nan gun base an tafi ko'ina ba,cikin yardar Allah Ubangijin halittu zaka kafa qafafunka harma ka samu daman yin sujjada da sunanSA"
ikon Allah,wai meye yasa hk ne,it's obvious,u really dont want to give me d support i deserve as an author,why is it dis hard to hear from u guys,kui min comment ko naa ji ra'ayoyinku!,ko ba don komai ba,don zemin sauqin sanin ko writeup dina na tfy yanda ya kamata,challenges din da nike jurewa both a ciki da wajena,crafting my feelings to words har in kawo maku bansan iya adadinsu ba,kawai dan bazasu lissafu bane,buh comment din da befi 'a single' line bane yake tamin wahalar samu har hk!,why mana,yeah,writing s' a hobby,nd dats d sole issue din dasuka sanya nike yi ma knn,nd so obsess to share dis feeling along with d mass,buh sam kun gaza bani motivation din da niketa buqata,which ponder me so so much,meye ya janyo hkn,seeking a single favour,repeating it over nd over again amman baa'a taba samun cigaba,ugh,leaving me with second thoughts on why not quit dis once nd for all,buddies,wallah ko 'tnx' dinku nike gani super means d whole world to me,wallahil azeem sosai nike baqinciki a kaf lokuta idan na dubi akwatin comment babu ko oho dinnan,it sulks me die,dan kawai bazaku san yadda nike ji bane,
emotional side of me,apologetic idan batutuwana sun bata ma waninku rai,no Malice,came straight from ma head plus hrt without filters,ur help with d votes nd comments pls

wa'annan suka kasance wasu cikin sautin lafuzzan dana jiyo ke tashen fitowa daga fatar bakin zahra,wanda ta kafe tanata faman bitansu da qwaqwalwanta (Hadda),kaman yadda ba kadai Alqur'ani take hadda ba,ya ha'da harda wasu muhimman littafan addinimmu,a shirye take tsaf shigar fita islamiyya,unnecessary motsin da taketa jiyowa marasa qara ne ya sanyata hanzarin setawa gun da take jiyosu,kaman yadda hasashenta suka bayar khairat ce nan durqushe site din da shoe rack dinta yake,ta wani maida kai se kace wadda aka aiko,banda bankade bankade da lalube laluben tarin takalman da ke gun babu wani abinda tasa gaba,
"_wai fa ki fadamin ke wacce irice ne,gasar kwalliya ake zuwa yi islamiyanne ko ko karatu,d worst part shiriritan naki be tsaya a iya nan ba,a kullum naki stuffs din baasu taba isanki,har se kin sa idanunki takan abin wani ko",furucin dasuka fito bakin zahra knn,a fusace ta qarqaresu da auna doguwar tsaki taja,
"kai fa Yaya,wai idan bakii sharing stuffs dinki dani ba to fadamin dasu waye zaki rabasu ne,nd nasan at d end of d day wa'annan duka de will be all mine de ko,
hamdulillah we wore thesame size,kuma de na tabbata komai qyashinki de qarshen abin tfy zaki ki barsu,if u no marry u go die fa,nd banda abunki keda a kullum ga ya Ya Najib pampering dinki kawai yake tayi da wa'annan abubuwan,dan kawai na dauki common 'Wedge' cikin tarin wa'annan se kuma ya zama abin ai min masifa",
a fusace zahra ta yunqurota da fadin,"ni din nake maki qyashi da masifan wato",yayinda khairat din ta fice da gudu gudu riqe da pair din takalmi a hannu,
tai qwafa a cikin ranta na jinjina how annoying siblings could forever be,dukkuwa da cewan tasan they are her most special enemies she just cant help loving,cant live without,nd her one nd only BFFS like no other,
ta koma ta zube mazaunanta gefen gado tana kuma jin wani emptiness kaman an zare mata wani muhimmin sinadari a jiki,wanda ya kasance kaman wani garkuwa ne dake mata katanga a tsakaninta da duk wani bacin rai ko alhini,duka ba komai bane suka taru suka hassasa wannan illa rashin jin sautinsa tun kawo i jiya da dare har i zuwa yanzunnan,nd all d thanks goes to those annoying twinning siblings of hers,afra da affan wa'anda a jiya jiyannan kamin su kwanta giggiwa da rashin natsuwansu har ya sanya suka sa qafa a kan saman wayanta suka take,yasa suka nakasta ilahirin screen din wayan raqwarqwafe,dan qarewarta ma tun incident din ko kunnuwa ma ba'a ci sa'a yayi ba,
a sannan ne kaman wadda ta tuna abu,ta sauke dubanta nan qasa ta gefen closet dinta,maaka makan paper bags ne har guda ukku,wa'anda Najib ya bar mata a haduwar da sukai jiya,wadda tun zamanin data zubesu gun bama ta kuma bi takansu ba,"uhm,su betterhalf kam dangin hidima",ta fada all smiles a karo guda se yunqurawan datai ta janyosu,wash,lalle fa kam,idanuna da bakina duka ware ne na ringa kallon abin arziqin da zahra ta bada azama tana fiddowa,box box,packs packs,da foils din da aka killace tarkacen snacks da chips din MC DONALDS ne suka somai min sallama,ga kuma conoid box din Chocolates,na brand din Debauve & Gallais,a dangin motsa baki fa,dangin tufafi ko,se kuma ga galla gallan Abayoyi masu qiran dubai har kala biyu,masu kalan skyblue da sea green wanda a qalla ko wanne dayansu ze iya haurawa sama da 100k,hadaddun takalma guda biyu na jimmy choo dana Gucci,wasu shegun handbags suma set biyu,na Fendi se na Hermes,duka match ne da kalan Abayoyinta,ga wasu kyawawan agogon gold kala biyu na Cartier La Dona,da wata 'yar qunbulalliyar make up kit na Mary Kay,ga tsadaddun perfumes biyu,na Chanel Grand Extrait da na masu abun wato AMP eau de cologne,wadda aka qawata shi na gaske,kama daga silvery flacon(kwalba) din turaren bayyane da qayataccen tambarin sunan masoyan wato NajRah,har ban ida birkicewa ba se dana tsinkayi kwalin danike kyautata zaton na wayane riqe hannunta,"ikon Allah,wai meye ya hau kan mutuminnan ne,Haba all these re more than necessary mana",zahra ta fada sa'ilin data saurara tana bin kayan da ido a tsanake,cikin wani irin yanayi dan kam lamuran Najib har sun soma qure mata tunani,a karo guda sabuwar waya fil fil me qiran iPhone XS ta sumbule,zuciyarta fari qal har ta kwashe tarin kayan ta maidasu cikin paper bags din,banda iPhone din dake hannunta,tarwatsatstsen galaxy s9 din dake kan dresser dinta ta janyo ta cire sim cards da memory dinta,take a lkcn ta sama masu muhalli a space dinsu na jikin iPhone din,ta kunna,babu abinda ta soma se dialing din layin Najib,
har seda sukai musanyen salon gaisuwa irintasu din da suka saba,sa'ilin zahra ta qara da fadin,"betterhalf kam wai baka gajiya da hidima ne,wa'annan kayan fa re way too much mana",
"shush,dont ever mention dat",
Najib ya fada a taqaice,sa'adda ya sauke numfashi ya canza wani zancen da fadin,"lfy,tun fa lokacin sallah'n fajr har kawo i yanzun i've been calling up ur phone endlessly turn off,which is so unlike u",
"wlh lfy fa,kai de ka bari kawai,tun jiya ne affan daya dauki wayan garin shirmensu ya fada cikin qasan cushion,har fa se dazun Allah yasa na iya daukowa,bada 'yar qaramar wuya bama",tai qarya domin real fact din anan shine sam baza taso yaji batun cewan wayan daya bata just less than 1month knn ya tashi aiki kawai dan careless nature irin nata,
'dan gajeren murmushi ya shimfido gefe dayan lebensa,kuma yai hamdala yace,"bakisan halin da kika jefani ciki bane wlh,like seriously,wlh i thought i'd die sbd rashin jin ki,frankly made me realise more how deadly m gonna be without u,har banison nai tunanin yadda zan iya jure even a single day pass ba tareda naji duriyanki ba",
"wlh nima same here fa"
"babe nasani ai,to hows' my heartbeat doing,meye da meye kikai yau,Allah de yasa baki wahalar min da kanki ba",
firarsu suka dan taba daga bisani suka ijje waya bayan da Najib ya sheda mata a kan zezo anjima,yazo dede da fadowan afra cikin dakin,"yaya wai kizo inji Abbammu",
wani irin qwalolo idanu zahra tai,take se ga wasu irin annuri na amsa kiran da akai masa,dan kallo daya zakai mata a lkcn ka kammala auna irin mashahuriyan farincikin dayai mata ado kaama daga can qasan zuciyarta har da bullowan dayai ya bayyana kansa a kan fuskanta,"Alhamdulillah" ta fada a rai tana kuma kitstsima irin farincikin da Najib ze yi a cikin daqiqun da take tsaka da fayyace masa wannan kyakkyawan albishir din,wanda ke tafe da cewan plow ahead,u have d blessing,an baka izinin da kake ta son samu na neman auren yarinyarnan da kake mutuwar so,da hanzari tai saurin dartse zaren bazawarar tunanin da ta faro,a karo guda tana kafe dubanta ga afra din dake tsaye gabanta,
cikin fara'a da doki ta daura hannayenta biyu kan saman kafadun afra tace,"yauwa my afryy,ai hala yananan parlor ko",afra ta murmusa cikin wani irin magana me kama da ra'da tace,"eh yananan dashi da umma yanzunnan ya gama cin abinci",
a qagauce ne zahra tai switch off din wayan dake hannunta,sannan ta jonashi da jikin charger,ranta fes a cikin hasashen atlast ga Abba nan ze bama soyayyarta da Najib cikakken 'yanci,ze bashi daman ya yunquro ya nemi aurenta,but what the hell,dukkuwa da cewan bawai tana da wani takamemen hujjar data sanya har tunaninta ke aron bakin Abba da ci masa albasa har hk ba,kawai dan wannan shine nan abinda makauniyar zuciyartata ke tsaka da kitstsimo mata ne nan,
har se data gama ayyane ayyanenta ta gama sa'ilin ta miqa ma afra hannu sukai 'high five' sannan ta kamo hannunta ta ruqo suka fice suka bar dakin so full of life,
Najib~5:35:56pm,ya fado a dede daqiqan da yai wani salon qayataccen murmushinsa a gun,ya sa hannu ya zare baqin Shade din dake manne da idonsa,idanun dake kafe kan kyakkyawar halittar data kasance masa rai daya tak tamkar da duniyar ma gabaki daya,a lkcn da ace zaka dubi birnin zuciyarsa lamuran da yaketa faman ayyanawa kanta ba masu adadin kwatance ba,qasaitaccen takunnata,me tafe da natsuwa,da kamewa ne ke kuma tfyr da imaninsa,idanunsa suka wani narke a cikin qarema tauraruwar halittarta kallo,yana kuma jaddada ma ransa a kan batun da yake tafe da cewan babu gudu babu ja da baya,yananan har se yaaga afkuwan ranan,a cikin awan,mintina har daqiqun da za'a shafe masu fatiha dashi da ita matsayin ma'aurata,bi'iznillah
isowansu dab gaban inda yake jingine da baqar motarsa BMW X6 ya taimaka akan tsinka masa igiyar tunani,kuma a tashi daya ne tarin annurin dake sanye kan fuskansa suka bace 'bat,aka nemesu aka rasa,ata dalilin cin karon da yai da yanayin damuwa da zullumin dake shimfide a qarqashin zuciya da saman fuskan zahra,tsayuwan datai gabansa turus ne har ya tilasta ma narkakkun idanuwanta yin kacibus a cikinnasa,wani zubin kallon dake tafe da isadda labaran zuciya,sukai barazanan birkita ma Najib dukkanin lissafi,har suka samu galaban sagar masa da ilahirin qarfin dake a cikin zuciya,ruhi da gangar jikinsa,wanda ma'auninsu ke a tafe da sanar masa cewan ba lfy ba,har be idda kidimewa ba seda yaga ta fashe da wani raunanniyar kuka ta wuce cikin gida wuf da iya gudunta
~~~"Ummi,karan kanki kinsan kaf duniyarnan baza'a taba haifan wani mahaluqin daya isa ya kaimu son ganin tafarkin rayuwanki na tfy bisa kan turba madaidaiciya,wannan yasa sam babu yadda za'ai mu runtse idanu har mu lamunci al'amuran daka iya zuwa su nemi su gurgunta maki rayuwa ummi,dan idan har na zuba idanu afkuwan hkn ta kasance bazan taba yafe ma kaina ba,sam ban cika uban daya amsa sunansa ba,magana nike takan batun alaqar da akwai tsakaninki da yaronnan Najib,bame bullewa bace,shidin be kasance managarcin mutum ba,ba kaman yadda dukkanimmu ke tsammaninsa ba,abin mamaki ko kadan babu ata fagen da yaron ya samu kyakkyawan sheda,dan hk wannan umarnine nan matsayina na wanda ya isa ya fada maki kiji,daga yau dinnan me kaman rana irin tayau,nake son ki shure duk wata dangantakar data taba ginuwa a tsakaninki dashi kina jina ko",
"ba se kin fada ba zahra'u,na gani kuma nasan kina qaunarsa,daughter inaso kisan ba so ne kawai madubi ba,nagarta,kyawawan dabi'un dake tafe da dabbaka mutunci da alfarma har da tsarin shari'an da addinimmu ya shimfida,wa'annan sune kan gaba,kiyi haquri kibi abinda mahaifinki ya gindaya,mu duka bamu isa munsan abinda Rabbi ke nufi ba,fatammu din shine ubangiji ya saka mana da zabi mafificin alkhairi,ki tashi ki tafi makaranta,Allah ya hada kowa da rabonsa",
zantukan mahaifanta ne suka ringa dawo mata daya bayan daya,a cikeda rudani ta kafe tana juyasu dalla dalla a cikin qwaqwalwanta,dukkuwa da cewan a iyanan kalaman nasu suka tsaya,har sun qagara sama ma kansu tasiri a ko daa miskinin tsoka ne na zuciyarta,dukkuwa da cewan sosai taketa son ta gwada bin umarnin mahaifanta,a lkcn har tanason ta bude baki ta fada masu cewan Najib din da suke magana a kai Najib din DA can ne ba nata na yanzun ba,amman ina,girman da iyaye ke dashi a tsabar idon zahra har sun kaita munzulin da babu wai yadda za'ai suna wannan maganan itama ta bude nata bakin tana kawo masu nata,ko kuma su shimfida mata wata doka ko iyaka ta nemi ta musanta su,Allah ubangiji ya tsareta da ganin irin wannan rana,amman gashi duk wani yunqurin da take tayi se zuciyar tata ta gaza bude mata qofar da zata jefar da soyayyarsa,batasan dalilan da suka sanya har zuciyar tata ke neman ya rinjayeta,sam bata hangi yadda za'ai Najib ya fita ba,da'ace Allah zesa ta maida hannun agogo baya,da tun wuri bata biyema tafkin zuciyarta ba,da tabi tunani da hnklnta,tasan da makamanciyar wannan ranar da taketa tsoro bata bijiro ta risketa,ranan da yake neman yai mata barazanan tsige wannan ingantaccen laqabinnan nata na "'Diya tagari"
daddadan qamshin mutumin data jiyo ne har ya taimaka a gun tsamo ta daga gungumin kogin tunanin data dulma,a tafe da taushin amon sautinsa wanda ke rera sallamar addinimmu kaman yadda su khairat sukai masa iso har a cikin gidan,a sittin take a lkcn gabanta yai wani irin mummunan yankewa ya fadi,har batasan sa'ilin datai wani wawan yunqurawa da zumman ficewa parlor'n wai da nufin kada ya shigo ya taddata,kadata qetare umarnin mahaifinta,ina,ba tareda ta ankara bane cikin rashin sa'a se jinta tai ta rufe da saman faffadan qirjinsa,cak numfashinta suka tsaya,a karo guda tana kuma jin yadda sautin qirjinta da nasa din ke cigaba da tsananta dukan lugude,daddadan qamshin turarensa na kuma bugan hancinta,daga nan ya samu kafar bin duk wata ga'ba ta jikinta,a hade da saukar mata da wani irin kasala me matuqar dadi,ta tsinci kanta da kuma narkewa jikinsa,kawo i yanzun bangaren Najib nasa alamuran sosai suka dame nata suka shanye nesa ba kusa ba,a halin da suke a yanzun shi kadai yasan salon shauqin daketa faman gudanyuwa mamaye a duk wata kusurwan loko da saqo na jikinsa,
ganin abinda ke faruwa bame cikakken inganci bane,yasa ya ringa qoqarin yin dagu da son zuciyarsa,har se daqyar ya iya jajircewa ya qwato rabin hnklnsa,wanda ya taimaka a dede lkcn ya raba jikinsa da nata,har ya bude bakinsa zeyi magana da zumman ya bata haquri kan abinda ya faru yanzun kuma de abu ya gagara,
"Najib,inaso ka daukarmin alqawari,dan Allah kamin alqawarin zaka tsaya tsayuwar DAKA ma soyayyar mu,i belief in u daka cemin u've changed ur no-good ways,kaman yadda ka jajirce a kaina,dan Allah kada ka gaza har se ka gamsadda Abbana kaaji,wannan ne kawai abinda zaka iya gwada min ka nunamin irin son da kake man,ka fadamin bazaka taba bari su rabani da kai ba
",cikin yanayin hargitsi ne Najib yasa hannu ya razana tarin suman dake kansa,kalamin datai na qarshe ne suka dirammasa kaman saukar aradu,cikin yanayin tashin hnkl ne ya iya taran bakinta,"wai meye yake faruwa ne,meye kike fa'da hk,bangane abinda kike nufi ba,ki fadamin da Allah,suwaye suke son su raba ki dani
",yadda yaga wasu kafaffun hawayen da suka gaji da tsiyaya ma fuskan zahra kaman famfo ne ya kuma ninka masa tashin hnkl,ruwan hawayen da a dazun ta nema ta rasa,sune nan a yanzun suke tsaka da bayyana kansu,tanajin wani irin abu qososo a tokare da qirjinta,jimami da jajen da takeyi na yadda zata iya jure rayuwa bayan rabuwanta da Najib ba dan qarami bane,so hana ganin laifi,dan sam kama daga idaniyanta,ya haura sama zuwa qwaqqwalwanta,ya kuma gangaro zuciyarta,suka gagara gaskata mata batun wai Najib dinta ba mutumin arziqi bane,ba de wannan din dake tsaye gabanta ba,
ta datse tunaninta,sa'adda ta daga kai tana auna dubanta a kansa,a saman fuskan sa ne ta tsinci hautsinannun kallo masu dauke da alamomin tmby,
farin hanky din dayake miqa mata ta amsa a taqaice,sa'adda suke kuma shagaltar da junansu da wani irin kallon da su kadai suka san ma'anarsa,ya sakar mata irin wimpy smile dinsannan da ko waye ya gani yasan ma'auninsa har yafi kuka ciwo,yadan tako ya rufe tazara kadan a tsakaninsu,har suna jiyo dumin saukar numfashin junansu,bugun zuciyarsu na qaruwa,cikin wani salon yanayi me tsumar da zuciyar masoyi ya kuma narkar da idanunsa a cikin nata,a dede lkcn wani irin 'dan gajeren hawaye ya fado daga cikin idanunsa,muryarsa ya karye da fadin,"hey,some kind of trouble in paradise right",
dede ga'bar da wani irin zazzafar sonsa ya kuma dirammata,soyayyar da iyayenta suka riga da suka haramta mata,
jinjina masa kai tai kaman zatai magana,sede kuma ta qiya,ata sakamakon wani gagarumin kukan daya qwace mata,a birkice ta ra'ba ta gefensa ta fice dakin,tashi daya ne sautin kukanta me qarfi yabi ya addabi duk wani sukunin dake cikin gidan,kuma yai dede da fadowan Abba gidan
sunnysmiles,UMMYSAUDAT

18_
Kai dakata,ni babu wani abinda zan ji daga gareka,'ya de diyata ce ko,kuma ni din ke da alhaki na za'ba mata mijin aure,managarcin mutum me kyawawan halaye da dabiun da suka saje da ra'ayina,to sam kai din baka shiga cikin jerin wa'annan mutanen ba,tun wuri gwamma ka janye duk wani quduri naka akanta,can ka tafi gun ire iren mata masu salon dabi'unka,ni kam bade da 'diyata ba,babu yadda za'ai na aurar da 'yata ga mashayin giya kuma ga dan iskan mutumin dayai qaurin suna irinka,na hada ka da girman Allah tun muna sheda juna daga yau dinnan kada ka sake kayi gangancin da har ze sani ganinka da ita ko alamunka a cikin gidana
"
duniyarsa ke juyawa a cikeda tsananin zugin radadi ne har ya himmatu da tariyo munanan lafuzzan da kunnuwannasa suka kammala jiye masa kimanin awanni uku ciff baya,yananan cikin motansan dake killace ta gefe can da jikin qofar gidansu zahra,inda ya zubar da kansa tun zamanin da ikon Allah ya fitar dashi daga cikin gidan,na ganosa da'bar mutuwar zaune saman seat me mazaunin driver,babu wani qwaqqwaran motsi a tattare dashi,banda azababbun ruwan qwallan dana gani na tsaka da silalowa kyakkyawan fuskansa,wanda shine kurum abinda ya bani sheda na alaman dakwai rai a tattare dashi,wanda rabon daya shiga makamancin hali na uqubar data hassaso masa zubarsu har ya mance shekarar,daga shi se Allah suka san tsananin alhini da tashin hnkln da suka taru sukai masa rufdugu a wannan lkc,wanda yake jin kaman ana tsaka da watsa ma ko wacce ga'ba ta jikinsa wuta ne,kai barimma ace masifaffiyar abar da kenan qulbuce can a qarqashin tsakiyar qirjinsa,wanda yake jin kaman ya 'kwaqulo ta ya zubar uban kowa ma ya huta,yake ma kansa addu'ar dama ace mutuwa ta iso tai awon gaba dashi,shi ze fiye masa gata dan gamuwansa da baqaqen ranakun dake tafe da barazanan rashin zahra,"Innalillahi
","Allahumma ajirny fy musibaty
","Qala rabbish rahly sadry
","Wa yassirly amry
",fal rudani ya ringa innatawa qasan zuciyarsa,sa'ilin da a hargitse ya zaro waya ya hau kiran layinta,da hk ya shafe wadataccen lkc batareda samun nasara ta kan abinda yake nema ba,kansa ya dauki caji,zuciyansa ya kuma bugawa da qarfi kaman me shirin faso qirjin ya fito,"shkn a yanzun zahra ba huruminsa bace!,da gaske ne nan ya rasata a rywrsa!",al'amuran da suka qwace ma qarfinsa ne yasa besan cikin daqiqun daya 'daga wayar dake hannunsa sama ba,"NO,dis cant be",ya doki steering dake gabansa da wani uban qarfi a hade da 'bare baki kaman wani bijimin zaki ya saki irin gigitaccen ihun daya sani falfalawa da gudu har ina neman na saki fitsari,wanda har seda motan yai wani wawan girgiza,abinka da mutumin da besan da zaman wai,"yana son abu ace an hanasa ba",lamuran suka zo masa a wani irin yanayi na wuju wuju,ai a haukace naga ya sama motar wuta,a hade da juya steering yai wani irin mugun u~turn,ya figa da mahaukacin gudu kai kaace sabon kamu,Allah me iko,bahaguwar hnkl da tunanin Najib baa su suka samar masa da akalar qaqqautawa ba har se da ya samar ma kansa wurin parking dede gaban wani hamshaqin Night Club din da kana gani kasan ba qananan miyagun qwari ne ke baje kolin ziyaransu gun ba,gabaki daya lamuran duniyan na cinsa ne ya 'ballo murfin motan ya fito kai tsaye se farfajiyan filin daze sada shi da cikin club din,kaman yadda rudin zuciya take dibansa a game da yaqinance masa cewan zuwansa wurinnan ne kurum abinda ze mantar dashi wannan tsatstsauran lamarin dake masa barazanan zautar da ilahirin hnkl da tunaninsa,se gashi saman wata doguwar stool din dake fuskantan Bar counter din gun,har beiyi wata wata bane yasa aka cika masa Wine cask fal da Whiskey din dayai ordering,sede kuma mei,'dagawan dayai ze kai bakinsa ke da wuya ne se ga kunnowan wasu batutuwa nan,a tashi daya suka karyo suka bugi saman qwaqwalwansa,"wai shin meye asalin fa'idar!,wacce irin musibar ce wannan yake neman ya kuma jefa rywrsa!,ina ribar dake a cikin zuwansa gurbataccen wurin nan!,shin anya wannan yabi hanyar da zata 'bullar dashi kuwa,sei meye akai knn idan ya kusanto kansa ga komawa gidan jiya,meye zesa ya kuma ha'b'baka kallon rashin cancantar da ake masa,meye zesa baze natsu ya fuskanci matsalarsa ta ingantaccen siga ba,",sannu a hnkl najib ya ringa qididdige munaqisar da shedan keson ya kuma shirga ma rywrsa,jikinsa ya mutu murus da sauke wine cask din Kaman yadda kwanaki biyar suka faru suka shude,se suka ha'da har afkuwan Ranan da mahaifin Zahra ya tarbi baqoncin Alhaji Ahmad Mekudi (meturare),kwatsam babu zato bare tsammani se fa ga uban daya haifi Najib har a Cedarcrest hospitals Abuja,sam dr Mukhtar naAllah bei mamaki da ganinsa hk ba,hasalima shirye yake tsaf da zuwannasa,dan kawo i yanzun babban abinda yai amanna dashi har qasan ransa shine batun ko daa gaba ki daya bainan mutanen duniyan zasu far masa,to babu ko gudan mahaluqin daya isa ya saukesa a kan dokin naqin daya hau,baza ya taba lamunce ma duk wani mutumin daze zo da niyyan ya gur'bata masa iyali ba,bazei ta'ba rumtse idanu da sakacin barin 'diyar daya haifa ta doshi muguwar hanyan cutuwa ba,kuma har wannan din babu abinda ya sakaye ma Alhaji,a inda shima ya kafe bil haqqi a gun fahimtar dashi asalin tsaftatacciyar son da 'dansa kema zahra,ko qalilan Najib bei shigo rywr 'yarsa da wani mugun quduri ba,daga nan ne har lamura suka samu kafar bankado kansu,sosai cikin girma da cikar dattaku Alhaji har ya gwanance sosai sukai magana ta gsky da fahimta a tsakaninsu,dukkuwa da cewan shine ya kawo Najib doron duniyar sam wannan bei sashi musanta munanan dabi'un da aka fasalta na 'dansa ba,amman a abinda ya faru ya wuce knn

wanda hkn yasa har besan sa'ilin da yabi ya shagaltar da dubansa a gun qarema kyakkyawan labbantan da aka kuma qawatawa da pink lippy mayen kallo ba,
qirjinsa na 'dan bugawa yai jarumtan dauke idanuwansa gun,
"hey m sorry,i let my emotions get d best out of me ne,ko kadan i've never meant even a single word kinji,kiyi haquri",yai zancen cikin wani irin tattausar sigar daya sata nemi fushin da take masa nan take ta rasa,

"ai naji kuma,amman shine a jiya kai tafiyanka ai,baka ko tsaya munyi sallama ba,har kasa ni kwana na tashi da rashin jinka ko daa a waya ne,ka jefa zuciyata a damuwa cikin tunanin ko kaima 'din zaka gujeni ni ne dan sbd
"tana kaiwanan ne se ta qagara samar ma zancen data soma aya ba,
"dan sbd meye zahra,batun fyaden da akai maki ko meye",
ya fadi zancen kamar fa bashi yayi su ba,a karo guda idanuwansa lumshe,ya auna wani irin wawan numfashi ya sauke,daga shi se Allah kadai suka san abinda yake ayyanawa a lkcn,can ya bude ya saukesu saman fuskan zahra wanda tuni zubar ruwan hawaye suka gama wanke mata,zuciyarsa na harbawa ya 'dan matso dab da ita ya kuma seta yana tsane mata su da taimakon farin hanky din dake hannunsa,"pls ki bar zubar man da tsadaddun ruwan hawayennaki hk,wlh it makes me feel more nd more guilty,ko ka'dan ban hangi wani dalilin dazesa ki damu kanki ba,inace ni ne nan zan aureki,kuma naji na amince,so zahra pls kimin alqawarin daga yau dinnan u will forgive nd forget all those fucking shits okay?
"

"ban gane abinda kake nufi ba",ta tambayesa cikin rashin fahimta,
kaman ze ce abu kuma de ya fasa,se ya cije lebensa na qasa yace,"never mind,it doesnt matter"

"ya dan 'bata fuska,"buh seems i d have to wait too long har nan da tsawon watanni ma
"
tsuke fuska tai da watsa masa manyan idanunta masu sheqin walqiya,"nd where's dat coming from,kaa jika fa,just two months dinne abin magana,ni da har nike ganin kamar ya matso kusa ma dayawa",

batai saurin amsa ba tace,"meye zanyi da katin ATM kuma",ta fada idanunta akan katin,
"kema kinsan abinda akeyi dashi",
"ni kam babu abinda zanyi dashi",ta fada tana zumb'uro bakinta gaba,
wani irin kallo ya watsa mata wanda a take ya sata shan ruwan jikinta,"kije ki debiting duk wani amount din da kikeso a duk sa'adda buqatar hakan ya taso,nd magana ni keyi matsayina na mutumin da zaki aura,nd kuma baki isa kiceman bazaki karbi abin hannun mijinki ba",(aha,lalle kam su miji manya),batai gigin kuma musantawa ba takai hannunta ta amsa,har ta bude baki da zumman tai magana amman ta maidashi ta tsagaita,ata sakamakon kakkausar amon sautin loudspeaker din dake fitowa kai tsaye daga babban masallacin unguwannasu,wanda yake fidda kiran faralin sallahn magrib
da hk 'din de suka haqura suka rabu bafa don a son ransu ba,yauwa,se don ya kamasu a dolen dolia ne,a inda suka rabu da alqawarin dayai takan zei dawo anjima bayan sallahn isha'i,Insha Allah,kaman yadda ya kuma sheda mata cewan dakwai batutuwan da yakeson zasu tattauna a gameda al'amuran da suka alaqanci bikin aurennasu

21_
Tun ana sauran sati hudu ai biki ne aka tattaro aka kawo ma zahra gagarumar lefe,boxes din akwatuna ashirin,wanda aka killace wasu irin ubansun ubansun din latest kaya masu masifar kyau da qarshen tsada,kuma na agani a fada,dan kam duk wanda yazo ya gani se ya tafi yaje ya bada labari,lefen da aka kawo hade da wata arniyar mota me qirar Ferrari F60 America kalarta silver,shima ga final exams din su zahra na session din Year2-2nd semester har se da bikin ya rage sauran sati ukku ne a sannan cikin yardar ubangiji suka kammalashi,wanda yake dede da qarqare karatunta na National Diploma knn,se fa a wannan lokacinne ta samu full time da sararin maidawa takan sabgogin na bikinta,a kullum itace surbing courses din da suka alaqanci cooking recipes da wasu stuffs din da suka shafi make up de,wata 'yar bare bari ce nan shahararriya kuma qwararriya Umma ta dauko mata,kasancewan sosai aka sakar mata da 'ya'yan banki se ya zama ba qaramin gyaran jiki ne ake barar ma jikin amaryar tamu ba,kama daga wanda take sha,na turarawa,na shafawa na wanka duka babu a inda akabar masakar tsinke,se hkn yasa cikin 'dan qanqanin lkc kam Amarya aka fito shar shar da ita tubarkallah abin fa se wanda ya gani,bangaren Ango kam zo kaga tsabar zumudi da 'dokin da ake tayi na ganin wannan babban rana,kai kaa ce ma akansa za'a soma mallakan 'ya mace,su Mahmoud kam babban aboki shima de ga aiki nan fa ya samu,dan babu irin gayyar jama'ar da ba'a jajubo ba,isassun gayu masu ji da asalin class da al'amuran da akema laqabi da qwalisa da tunqahon quruciya,abinka da dama shi Najib din ba daganan ba,itama bangaren zahra ananan anata aikin rabon IV,sede a cikin sharuddan da Abban zahra ya shimfida ma Najib,dakwai wanda ya buqaci da shi da zahra din su tafi asibiti sui General lab test,duka ba da wata manufa ba illa don hnklnsa ya kuma kwantawa da al-amuran shi Najib din,taimakon Allah yasa sam ba'a samu wata matsala ba,kama daga bangaren Najib ballantana kuma zahra,domin kua ko zamanin da yai taken abinda ake cema iskanci sam be taba gigin saduwa da mace babu amfanin protective ba,kaman yadda asalinsa dama a kullum shi me rigakafi ne kan duk wani abinda ze shafi lfyr jikinsa ko a wani hali ne,haka din akai ba tareda wani matsalar ba se gadan gadan aka kacame da shirye shiryen biki,a ko ta ina babu sauqi,yazama gabaki daya kafofin watsa labarai a fadin qasar Nigeria ya dauka babu trending news din daya wuce na bikin auren 'da a gun attajirin dan kasuwannan Najib,dangin yan uwa da abokan arziqi duka an zama ready dan kam abin na jigai jigai ne,da hk lkc nata qaratowa har aka soma events din biki,tun ana sauran sati daya daurin aure ne aka soma,inda Najib yai bachelor party da mutanensa,a gefen zahra itama tai nata bachelorette party din da girl gang dinta,daga bisani akai bridal shower,Dinner ya biyo baya,a ranar wata Juma'a da qarfe biyu dede na rana a cikin babban masallacin Ali Bn Abi Talib din garin Kano ta dabo ne yardar ubangiji da hukuncinsa ya qaddara daurin auren Najib Ahmad Mekudi da amaryarsa Zahra Mukhtar NaAllah,akan sadaki dubu dari laqadan ba ajalan ba,daurin auren daya samu halartan dumbin jama'a da manya manyan mutane ako ta ina na qasar dama wajensa,wa fa ya gano ango da 'dan qaramin bakinnan nasa har kunnuwa
Reception na walima akai hosting bayan daurin aure,Washe gari asabar da yammacin Allah ta'ala bataliyan motocin abokanan ango ne a ko ta ina bakin qofar gidansu zahra,unguwa tai tatul da cincirundun matasa maza da mata,abin yazo inji me tsoron wanka,anfa zo daukar ma ango amaryarsa,har se da iyayenta suka gwanance sukai ta mata salon tsaftatacciyar huduba da nasiharsu me ratsa jiki,abu fa kaman wasa de da hk din tana tirjewan tana kukan tana komai aka tattara aka dangana Gidado road a inda katafariyar Duplex house din Najib yakenan girke,anci ansha anyi buduri an kuma yi qarya har qarshe,yayinda kudade suka yi kuka kaman ba'asan wahalar samunsu ba,aka kammala komai lfy lfy taro ya watse Alhamdulillah,se ango da amarya aka bari dagasu fa se halinsu

3years leap,Shekaru ukku gaba,
AUSTRALIAya kasance a nanne Muhallin Najib yake da zama i war hk,kamar yadda dududu shekara guda bata shude ma aurennasa bane ya tattara da iyalinsa ya koma can transfer university of Melbourne da aikin professorship,daga nanne ikon Allah da tallafinSa ya bashi aron rai da lfyn hada aiki da karatu,part-time ne yai enrolling kansa wani business institute nan Australia din,tuquru ya maida kai ya kafe ya jajirce don ganin ya cimma cikar qudurinnasa,wanda yakeji tamkar nauyin bashi ne a kansa,kuma Falillahil hamd sosai ubangiji ya dubi manufarsa kaman yadda ya sabaima bayinsa ya kuma azirtashi da ilimin da yaketa nema,Masha Allah,kawo i yanzun sosai Najib yake ganin he is more than ready don ya farantama mahaifinsa rai,se yazamana a yanzun babu wasu lafuzzan da ke ta faman kaiwa da kawowa qarqashin farar zuciyarsa illa wanda yaketa innata tarin hamdala a tafe da fadin,"couldnt be more ready,nd for sure,for sureAMP!,here i definitely come"~~a yau din ta fa'do a Laraba,da yammacin Melborne city na qasar Australia,

~dukkuwa da cewan idanuwannata nanan a lullubene,se be zo a dede da cewan barci take ba,ta de tafi nisan kiwo ne a can qololuwan zurfin tunani,a nanne har nai karanbanin amfani da daman aron tunaninta da ci mata albasa,
Zahra's POV,
Allah qara ma Annabi ta'rin wasila da fadila,shakka babu,zancen Annabimmu Muhammad SAW ne ya tabbata,a inda yace,"Mubi iyayemmu,nd babu yadda za ai mu ta'ba kuskurewa",yeah,couldnt have been more proud of my self nd my faith in Allah,har dana iya tsallake wannan siradin,domin ko na sani,na sheda kuma na tabbatar da cewan albarkar sune ke ta faman dawainiya da rayuwata har ilaa yau 'dinnan,a kullum ni me alfahari dasu ne kaman yadda suke alfahari dani,ni 'yar albarka ce nan,kuma bazan ta'ba shayin na bugi qirji na furta wannan da babban murya ba,domin alal haqiqa ba don su ba i couldnt be d very person i am right now,couldnt have i been dis fortunate nd blessed,Ya Salam,ba'na tab'a manta marayan yanayin dana tsinci rywata cikin farar ranar da aka miqa ni izuwa muhallin mijin aurena,all those emptiness,those feelings din dana ringa ji tamkar an tsige man wani muhimmin sinadari ne daga jikina,so mixed up a cikin tunanin sabuwar rywr da zan iya daurewa ba tareda su ba,without dem in my watch,ba tareda 'yan uwana ba,ba kaman yadda nake kwana na tashi in a single plus a carefree life ba,har ya zama fargaban dana fada me matuqar gaske ne na yadda zan iya jure ma wannan sabon canji,my brand new self,a new life,a new home,matar wani ce nan a qarqashin inuwa da ikonsa,matsayina ta matarsa,matar da a yanzun igiyoyi da haqqoqin aure masu girma da daraja suka rataya kaina,wanda ko inaso ko banaso its a freaking deal i must live nd adapt a life in,dan ko ba jima ko ba dade nasan ala dole ne nai experiencing wannan lkcn a rywta,ko dan na samu sauqi yasani leaving it right in d back of my mind cewan kwana zan ringa yi ina tashi right next to d very same person i love most in my dear life,kuma na taki uwar sa'a se ban sha wani wahala ba,sbd Najib ne nan,wlhl azeem de da qwayar zarra be bar mani ko daa gudan dalilin daze sa ni shan wuyan rungumar sbwr rayuwata a tare da aboki,amini kuma masoyi irinsa ba,Masha Allah,i couldn't be more than happier,3years of marital bliss have been among d best nd most adventurous chapters of my life so far,i admit babu abinda yakai rayuwa da masoyi dadi,fortunately,rayuwar aure na have been bouncing so fair nd square,with Najib as a patience,endurance,understanding,trust,commitment nd all those haqqin ma'aurata stuffs de to make it work,nd indeed we've been working a great job,nd u know what all d thanks surely goes to Ubangijin daya haliccemu,Allah akbar da Ya sauqaqa mana komai da komai,a cikin dumbin bainan yan adam din daya halitto,He meant us to be,kamar yadda ya qaddara kyautatuwar dangantaka a tsakanimmu,a tafe da cusa mana tsananin so da qaunar juna,me tattare da tsuran shaquwan da a kullum kullu yaumin gaba gaba yake bei taba ci baya,dukkuwa da batun daya ce zamantakewar aure zo mu zauna zo mu sa'ba ne nan,sam duk da wannan bei hanemu daman riqe amanar da zukatammu ke kitsimawa ba,wanda yake ta faman jaddada mana batun daya ce 'no matter what' zamu kasance ne tamkar tsintsiya guda madaurinki daya,babu fa me jin kammu,kaman yadda ya kasance babu wani abinda ya isa ya hargitsa mu,nd dat makes an ideal family right?,d three of us nd our future bi'iznillah,yeah u got me,there's d three of us,a yanzun mu uku ne nan,with me,Najib nd our yet unborn child
~'dib a cikin daqiqa guda ne duk wani tunani nata ya tsaya cak,aiko nan 'daga idanuwanta keda wuya ne sukai caraf qulle acikin nasa,wanda shigowan nasa knn da sallama a qunshe da fatar bakinsa,bakinta washe ne ta amsa masa cikin tattausan lafazi karo guda tana a tsaka da mayar ma mijinnata martanin lallausan murmushin dake kuma bayyanar da zallan so da begensa,sanye yake cikin wata dakakkiyar Tuxedo Suit dinsa me kalar sararin samaniya,wanda tsaf yake hasko asalin kwarjinin dake tattare da zubinsa,sosai ya kuma shiga cikin sahun jerin irin mazajennan da sukaci suka qoshi kuma suke alfahari da tsuran gayu da kuma cikakkar qira da kyawun fasali,"oyoyo oyoyo",ta fada fal murna sa'ilin data ijje baby magazine din dake hannunta ta daddafa ta jikin kujera ko don ya bata taimakon gaggawan miqewa zumman ta iso ta tarbi rabin rannata,har be barta ta kaiga kammala manufar tata 'din bane ya hanzarta isowa gareta,a lkc guda ya cillar da briefcase din dake saqale kafadarsa da car keys harda paper bag din hannunsa bisa kan sofa,a sannan ya samu cikakken daman rungomo abarsa yana lumshe idanu,itama qanqamesa tai shiru a cikin faffadan qirjinsa banda shaqan daddadan qamshin cologne dinsa babu abinda take,dukkuwa da yanayin laulayin da aka sani na me ciki sam basu sanyata tsanarsu ba,

"hey dear,i'm sorry kinda late right?"ya ra'dama kunnenta a kaikaice,
murmusawa tai da fadin,"no dont mention that,kawai de Allah sa ba yanayin hayaniyan Uni bane suka hadu suketa wahalarman da miji ba",
dagota yai a nutse ya da'fo tsinin cikinta,"tab',wa yake ta ni ne kuma,kudai yaya jikin?,zahra fatan babu komai de"ya kammala zance yana binta da irin kallon dake nuna tsabar kulawa,
ta sauke boyayyen ajiyar zuciya,domin har ga Allah daga ita se mahaliccinnata ne kadai sukasan al'amuran dake dawainiya da gangan jikinta,wa'anda kuma sosai suke kuma sanya take jinjinama duk wata uwa a duk inda take,yayinda sabon salon so da qaunar tata uwar yake kuma daskare duk wata kusurwa da lungun zuciyarta,but what d hell,ai u know dat kinda weird feeling of striving it really hard enduring each nd every kind of suffering kawai dan kaa riga da kasan it worths all d trouble right?,to shinenan abinda zahra taketa faman jurewa,tana me qaqalo masa murmushi tace,"gamunan fa Masha Allah,nd trust me betterhalf idan nace maka har mun fika lfy ma",

"to yauwa sweetheart give me just 5 min",yai furucin da dage mata girarsa guda cikin sassarfa ya amshe rigar suit din dake riqe hannunta ya wurgar,ba tareda ta ankare bane taji ya dauketa cak ya zaunar dasu a saman 3seater da ita a cinyarsa,gigin tsananin 'dokin farinciki na dibansa ne yasa hannu ya dage rigar jikinta,wanda ya taimaka qwarai a gun bayyano farin fatar 7month baby bomb din tumbinta,kacokam ya bi ya shagaltar da dubansa kan cikin tamkar duniyarsa all depend on it ne,a tafe da wadatacciyar ajiyar zuciyar da ya sauke yasa tafin hannunsa gun yana shashshafawa,a cikin halin da duba daya zaka gwada yi masa ka fahimci salon qasurgumar shauqin so da qaunar da yakema gudan jinin nasa tun ma be kai ga fadowa doron duniyar ba,al'amarin daya sanya zahra lumshe idanuwa tana mai
