26_
da hk duniyar take juyawa,kuma al'amura da dama suke afkuwa har ma su shud'e su zama labari,a cikin ranakun da suka faru suka wuce na shafukan kundin qaddarar Najib ya had'a har da wanda ya karb'i sammaci daga State high court ana tuhumarsa da laifin kisan kan Mufidah Magaji Mabel,dukkuwa da yadda y'an uwa da abokanan arziqi sukai ta k'undunbalan ganin abin be kai labari ba,se ikon Allah ya kayar dasu qasa warwas,yayinda shi Najib d'in be nuna ko d'ar ba,sabida me?,yasan bashshi da wani dalilin da ze sa ya d'aga hnkl kan laifin daya tabbatar ba shine yai ba,ina! bei ci nanin ba nanin bazata ci sa ba,se ya jingine al'amuransa ya fawwalasu ga Allah huwal Aleemul Hakeem,da shike Allah ba azzalumin Sarki bane,'wa mallahu yureedu zulmal lil alameen',se ya kasance a zaman farko da akai kotu zuwa na biyu aka tara qwaaraaran shedun da suka wanke Najib fes a cikin ruwan sanyi,ba fa da taimakon wani ba,taimakon Allah da kuma taimakon CCTV camera na gidannasa ne aka bi diddigin al'amuran da suka wakana a ranar sha takwas ga watan yulin shekarar da ake ciki,wanda ya kama daga tataccen rashin mutuncin da Mufidah da qawayenta biyu,Ramatu da Azeemah suka surfa ma Zahra,har ya zuwa bayyanar Najib da fitan da yai riqe da zahra,dawowansa gidan daga bisani har da qaramar yaqin da sukai dashi da Mufidah,gashinan qiri qiri na'urar bata bar komai ba har lkcn da ta sakar ma kanta harsashin bindiga ya fasa mata kai har lahira,rashin qwararan shedu a gefen masu qara yasa akai watsi da complaint d'in na Brigadial Magaji Mabel,yayinda kuma ake tsammanin mutumin ze zagaya yabi duk wani hanyan da zebi don ganin ya huce baqincikin mutuwar y'ar tasa tilo se kuma fa labari ya juye ya sha ban ban,duka bada gudummowan ko wanne mahaluqin ba ne ba se na bawan Allahn da ake ma laqabi da Alhaji Ahmad Mekudi(meturare),Mahaifin Najib ya kasance irin k'waarin mutanennan ne masu baiwan iya sarrafa zance da kuma madaukakiyar girma da kwarjini a idon jama'a,akasari da wannan baiwar da ubangiji ya huwace masa ne yake zame masa makami gun saye zukatan jama'a,mutumin da ya dawo daga baya har a bakinsa kake jin kalmar "MA FATA FATA",toh babu mamaki ko watak'il da wannan ne yai amfani gurin narkar da zuciyar ta Brigadial Magaji Mabel,ai daga hk ne akalar rayuwar Najib ta miqa simiqal ba tare da wani tangarda ba,ata ko wanne b'angare bashshi da wani ragowan matsala,Najib ya zama babban mutum na qin qarawa,sosai Allah ya daukaka girmansa har a idanuwan jama'a,kamar yadda ya zamana yanzu hk kaso 75 bisa d'ari na operations d'in rukunan manya manyan kamfanonin AMP wanda ya kasance family business din da mahaifinsa ya kafa,duka a qarqashin iko da gudanarwarsa yake,baya ga hk Najib ya kuma hab'b'aka gidauniyar daya kafa tun shekara da shekaru idan me karatu me manta ba,domin tallafama al'umma marassa qarfi,da kuma wata gidauniyar tasa ta yaqi da shan miyagun qwayoyi a tsakanin matasa maza da mata,da hana zaman banza,Najib yaa kasance garkuwa ya kuma zama abin koyi ya yi shahura kan ayyukan alkhairinsa kuma abin koyi ga duk wani matashin dake tasowa a fadin qasar Nigeria dan har se daya samar ma dubban matasa aikin yi qarqashin inuwar mabanbantan rassunan kamfanonin AMP,a kwana kwanannan ya kuma kafa wata babbar cibiyar dake daukar nauyin jigilar kaiwa da kawowar al'umman musulmi marasa hali sauke faralin aikin Hajji,niyyarsa duk shekaraa bangaren rayuwar data shafesa da iyalinsa kuma,babu ata fagen da zaka tab'o su wai kace ka jiyo kansu,ba kuma wani abinne ya kasance masu garkuwa ba illa shaquwa da amintacciyar soyayyar da ubangiji ya halitto a tsakanin zukatansu,gaba gaba yake kuma yi yai nisa har ya fice ya kuma zarce tunanin duk wani mutum,yasa ko a kasantuwar ranar da zahra ta tsinkayi labarin da ya tabbatar mata da gaskiyar lamarin wai Najib dinnan de,mijinnata,abin alfaharinta shi ne nan ashe mutumin daya keta mata haddi ta hanyar fyade,amma fa a shud'ewar lokutan da rayuwarsa bata waye ba,yake kuma a cikin duhun da bega hasken da yake gani a halin yanzun ba,bata san abin daya makantar da ita ba,bata ga laifinsa ba,bata tab'a ganin baqinsa ba,ta rasa meye yasa,har ma take ganin shin wai ma ina ribar ne!,ina ribar da zata ci ne idan tai masa qyashin yafiyarta,alhakinta a kansa baze cutar mata dashi ba kua?,wannan baze shafeta ba kua
,haqqun, cutar Najib cutar ta ne nan,lfyn Najib lfynta ne,ko a wani hali ya tsinci kansa me kyau ko akasi dole ne su shafe ta
soyayyar da take masa ne nan yasa,yaa riga daya gama d'aukanta kacokam,a inda ta taki sa'a se be kaita wurin daze barota ba
,a gefe guda kuma yayinda Zahra take tunanin ita iyaa ilimi da kwalin karatunta na National Diploma(ND) sun isheta zaman duniya da mai da yaji,tashi guda se Najib ya shayar da ita mamakin da bata tab'a zato ko tsammani daga garesa ba,rana tsaka ya damqa mata admission letter nta na BUK Course din Pharmaceuticals,dukkuwa da cewan course din ya sha ban ban da wanda tai baya take kuma da burin ta lalubo aiki dashi wato SLT,se bata nuna masa ba,taje tai karatunta halftime,shekaru biyar rigis Allah ya nufeta da kammalawa,wanda acikin halin da ake ciki yanzu hk tuni Najib ya bud'e mata wani tamfatsetsen pharmaceutical industry,wanda za'a riqa had'a nau'ikan drugs ana distributing ma cosmopolitan da kuma wani Clinic gefe guda duka da sunanta,wanda ko qaddamar da bude su d'in ba ai ba tukuna a cewarsa wai se bayan Allah ya sauketa lafiya
da Farar Safiyar Laraba,wanda ya fad'o a ranar Ashirin ga watan Febrairun shekarar 2019 na kalandar bature,
Zahra_Lafiya,Kwanciyar hankali,Rufin asiri,abu mawuyaci a samu wanda ya had'a wa'annan,shekara d'aya,biyu,ukku,hud'u,biyar,shidda sun shude ma rayuwata,nd in every passing day i've always prayed for Allahs' blessing,ya Allah make my present more better than my past,better my future far more than my present,addu'ata a kullu yaumin be wuce wa'annan,nd yeah here i am,ba dabara ta bace ba,qaddara tace,Alhamdulillah gaba gaba nike kuma yi couldnt be more thankful to Allah (SWT),
"t-a-r-t-s" wani irin murd'awan da cikinta ya bayar qululu a tareda qaran tarwatsewan mug d'in dake riqe hannunta ne suka taimaka a gun tsinka mata zaren tunani,"Ya Rabb",ta fada firgigit tana d'an karkad'e wadatacciyar Arabian gown d'in jikinta fara tas,wanda ruwan shayin da take sha a mug d'in ya watse ya faffalatsa mata jiki,da kuma ta gode ma Allah fasassun tangarayen basu soki jikinta ba knn,a inda take nan zaune dining area ta d'an matsar da kujerar da take kai sa'adda wata hadimar dake ankare da abin da ya faru ta b'ullo ta gyara wurin,
kusan kamar yadda take shekarun baya hk take sede a yanzu ta d'anfi da can d'in nuna alamar qoshi da siffar irin matan manyan mutanennan,ta lumshe idanuwa da qarfi ta aza hannuwanta a saman tulelen baby bump dinta haihuwa yau ko gobe,wani irin zugin ciwo ne ke taso mata tun kama daga tumbin cikinnata ya zuwa qasan maranta,shi ba tsayayye ba shi ba tafiyayye ba,wanda ta fara jin some somensa tun shekaran jiya,dukkuwa da cewan ya so yai kamanceceniya da irin wanda taji a lokacin naqudan Abba,sede lissafin da yasa bata kawo kan Naqudan ne ba shine kasancewar EDD d'inta wata d'aya har da d'orin kwanaki 7,kawai laulayi ne,bata wani dauki abin babban da ze sata sanar ma Najib ba,ita ba ko da yaushe ne take maraba da wannan overprotective d'abi'ar tasa ba,k'asaitaccen qamshin turaren nan nasan de na Clive Christain No 1,shi ne abin da ya soma isar mata da labarin alamansa,kana se qyaqyatawan Ahmad din dake tunkaro jinta,sannan suka bayyana a gaban idanuwanta,sama tsakankanin wuyan Najib na gano Ahmad aze,sai faman wuwwuntsila qafafuwa yake tayi cikin shauqin murna,da uban da d'an yanayinsu na nuna babu wani matsalan dayai saura a fadin duniyarsu,gagarumar soyayyar dake tsakaninsu baya tab'a boye kansa a duk lkcnda suke tare,Najib a sanye yake tsaf cikin wani satiny Suit kalar grey,sak shigar tfy office,baki sake na ringa qareshi da kallo,sabili da canzawan da yai irin like wow dinnan,ya kuma tara wasu lafiyayyun qasumba,wanda ya qara ma zubinsa kyawu da kwarjini ainun,yayi fes dashi ya kuma yin wani b'ulb'ul abinsa fiye da da,nera yana aiki knn,irin manyan mazajennan wa'anda suka sa duniya a gaba kamar baza su tab'a barinta ba,kuma suke iyaa qoqarin yinsu don neman lahiransu a ciki,tfyrsa yakeyi ras kaman be taba samun wani matsala da qafafuwan ba,wanda har se mutum ya jima yana bin takunsa da kallon qurilla har ze lura da rashin daidaituwar tasu
ko dana komawa Ahmad AKA Abba,d'an da maniyyin NajRah ya samar knn kimanin shekaru biyar d'in da suka shude,uban masu gida wanda yaci sunan kakansa Meturare,nd have u guys in anyway noticed yadda iyaye suke alfahari suke jindad'i idan an mayar da sunansu,toh lalle Najib yana sane da wannan,kamar kuma yadda a kullum babu wani abin da yake alla alla yayi se wanda yasan ze faranta ran mahaifinnasa,Ahmad a sanye yake tsaf shigar uniform na makarantar boko,kamanninsa da mahaifinsa kamar an tsaga kara,harda chubbiness din jikin da komai na zubin fuskarsa irinna Najib,sede shi Ahmad fari ne irin hasken gyatumarsa,lol,tubarkallah kamar iri irin yarannan da company take nema ruwa a jallo don ayi advert ko a saka a Baby Mag,sosai inde kyawu ne akwai shi ba qarya,abu da daman a jininsa yake,nan suka tsiri breakfast da jerin nau'ikan ababen ci da sha d'in dake a saman dining table din,wa'anda suka kama daga manya manyan tumblers guda ukkun dake a cike dam da blackberry Smoothie,ga kuma serving tray din dake dauke da crystal jug din da yai fal da ruwan shayin Cold _Peppermint,mugs rabin dozen zagaye a gefensa,ga bowl d'in da aka cika Cheddar_Cheese sannan da wanin dayai fal da wheat Crackers,warmer din da suka bude suna serving ma kansu daddadan Spinach,Cheese and Tomato Omelette tururin qamshinsa ya taso ya bade ko ina,suna dab da kammala kalacin suka amsa ma Nanny d'in Ahmad excuse tana me tunasar dashi kan school driver d'insa yana ta jiransa kada ya kai ga makara,"Son where is your backpack,oyaa kawo min nan na gani",Zahra ta fad'a tana kallon Ahmad d'in da Najib ke taimaka masa da sauka a kan dogon kujerar dining d'in da yake kai,ya amsa mata cikin azama ya tafi ya karb'a a wurin Nanny ya miqa mata,yayinda yasa hannuwansa biyu ya kama qugu yana tsayar da hnklnsa da dubansa akan cikinta,irin kallonnan me tafe da alaman wai yaushe ne babynnan na cikin Cikin mommah ze faso ya fito ne,ko dan ya samu k'ani ko k'anwa,kamar yadda Amminsu Nuwairah(Raheelah) take ta fad'a masa da suka zo jiya tace masa yaa kusa samun k'ani ko k'anwa,se da Zahra ta gama inspecting ko ta ina na jakannasa tsaf,ta tabbatar babu wani abin daya kamata a gani ciki da babu,hk zalika babu abin da be kamata a gani ciki ba da akwai,sannan ta saqale masa a baya,tai amfani da hannuwanta ta juyar dashi yana fuskantanta tana me sakar ma d'annata murmushinta me cikeda qauna sannan ta matsa tai pecking both kumatunsa,tana saka masa albarka,tana yi masa hudumar nan na 'do and donts' d'in da aka san duk wata mahaifiya ta qwarai ke ma d'anta idan zashi Son zo nan naga"Najib ya fad'a hnklnsa a d'an tashe yayinda ya lura da wawulon gib'in haqoran d'annasa biyu na sama,ya kamo hannunsa har ya isa dab dashi,"haa bude min bakinnaka muga haqoran",Ahmad d'in daya soma tsorata da ganin damuwan dake kan fuskan mahaifinnasa yace muryansa kaman na wanda yake shirin kuka,"Daddy ba tun wannan jiyan bane ba da jiyan da ya wuce ba,yake ta gingindi yanata gingidi,shi ne ya fita na bawa mommah dan ta gani ta nunawa babymmu na cikinta,se anjima se naga ta bama nanny tace mata taje ta binne min shi,tace min wai wani ze fito,daddy dan Allah naje da nanny na dauko ka dawo min dashi daddy dan Allah ka dawo min dashi nasan baze fito ba
",yaron ya kawo zancen yana k'ok'arin fashewa da kuka,duka wannan drama n Zahra se idanuwan babu baka,dan kawo i yanxun ita kad'ai tasan abin da takeji,se kuma Mahaliccinta,da hk ne Najib ya shiga lallaminsa har ya tafi makaranta,haba ace b'anb'ara ga d'an da be wuce shekaru 5 ba,just way too early,toh ko buge haqoran yai,cikin ransa yana ayyana tun da yau d'in da wuri ze dawo aikin idan yaron ya dawo makaranta ze kira family Dentist d'insu yazo ya duba ko ma meye ne,da wannan ne ya share yana maida cikakkar hnklnsa ga Zahra,yana kuma lura da yadda take ta nishi tana yayyatsinewa tana ciccije lebe,"baby yaya de ko kin fara jin wani abu ne"yai zancen yana komawa kujerar kusa da ita wanda Ahmad ya tashi yana son yaji amsar da zata bashi,girgiza masa kai tai alaman a'a,dukkuwa da cewan ba wai tana da tabbacin amsan data bashi d'in ba,ya shafo cikinta yace da amon dake nuna tsabar tausayawa da kulawansa,"Angel to meye ne",had'iye miyau tai maqwat tana jin d'aci d'aci a bakinta,"betterhalf ni kada ka damu babu komai kawai ka kaini d'aki enaso na mik'e kafa na",ya miqe daga wurin da yake ya dauketa cikin ransa na waswasin ko ze fasa fita aikinne,se kuma ya tuna da yadda sukai da Alhaji yau da safennan a waya,wanda yake masa albishir kan da akwai wasu Investors d'in da suke son sui signing contract da AMP kuma VIPs ne za'a samu abin da ake so,sede sun buqaci su fa lalle se sun gana dashi Najib d'in tukuna gabanin hk zasu cimma matsaya ma kwangilar,wani irin abu da Zahra taji ya tsikareta bada wasa ba ne yasa bata san daqiqan da ta daddage ta tsala wani gigitaccen qara ba,"wayyo Allah cikina,marana,betterhalf ka taimakamin haihuwa zanyi",dede lkcn kake ganin wani ruwa shaaa a tsakankanin qafafuwanta,ruwan faya ya fashe,wanda se a sannan ne ta gane ainihin halin da take ciki,ashe lokacin haihuwanta ne yai ba tareda watannin sun cika ba,ai a tsure mutumin ya kuma qanqame matar tasa a cikin ruqonsa ya rarumi dan maqullin mota yana jera mata sannu da addu'o'in da yake tofa ma setin kunnenta "Hanna wulidat Maryam wa Maryam wulidat Isah ukruj aiyuhal maulud bikuditil ma'aruj_Ya Hayyu Ya Qayyumu bi Rahamatika astagisu" ya fita da ita yai asibiti,Allah mai girman iko,zuwansu asibiti da y'an mintinan da basu wuce sittin ba zahra ta sumb'ulo santalallun y'ay'anta tagwaye mace dana miji,masu balain kyau irinna iyayensu,har se da aka gyara su tsaf tsaf sannan akai dakin hutu dasu,Najib ya shigo rud'e da farinciki yana rawan jiki nan take ya daukesu yayi masu huduba,inda yaran suka ci sunan Zaid da Zaheeda,yayinda kuma addu'ar iyayennasu bei wuce Ubangiji Allah Ya albarkaci rayuwarsu,Ya karesu daga dukkan sharri,Ya kuma raya masu zuri'a har dama ta alumman musulmi bai daya
and they lived happily ever after,TAMMAT BIHAMDULLAH
